raunaqeshamesafar tabasahar sannata
qsimateshairesimabsifat dasht ki maut
qimaterezaealmasehunar sannata
janemohsin miri taqdir men kab likkha hai
dubta chand tira qurbegajar sannata

qatl chhupte the kabhi sang ki divar ke beach
ab to khulne lage maqtal bhare bazar ke beach
apni poshak ke chhin jaane pe afsos na kar
sar salamat nahin rahte yahan dastar ke beach
surkhiyan amn ki talqin men masruf rahin
harf barud ugalte rahe akhbar ke beach
kaash is khvab ki taabir ki mohlat na mile
shoale ugte nazar aae mujhe gulzar ke beach
dhalte suraj ki tamazat ne bikhar kar dekha
sarkashida mira saaya safeashjar ke beach
rizq malbus makan saans maraz qarz dava
munqasim ho gaya insan inhi afkar ke beach
dekhe jaate na the aansu mire jis se mohsin
aaj hanste hue dekha use aghyar ke beach

sanson ke is hunar ko na asan khayal kar
zinda huun saaton ko main sadiyon men dhaal kar
maali ne aaj kitni duaen vasul kiin
kuchh phuul ik faqir ki jholi men daal kar
kul yaumehijr zard zamanon ka yaum hai
shab bhar na jaag muft men ankhen na laal kar
ai gardbad laut ke aana hai phir mujhe
rakhna mire safar ki aziyyat sambhal kar
mehrab men diye ki tarah zindagi guzar
munhzor andhiyon men na khud ko nidhal kar
shayad kisi ne bukhlezamin par kiya hai tanz
gahre samundaron se jazire nikal kar
ye naqdejan ki is ka lutana to sahl hai
gar ban pade to is se bhi mushkil saval kar
mohsin barahnasar chali aai hai shamegham
ghurbat na dekh is pe sitaron ki shaal kar

saare lahje tire bezaman ek main
is bhare shahr men raegan ek main
vasl ke shahr ki raushni ek tu
hijr ke dasht men karvan ek main
bijliyon se bhari barishen zor par
apni basti men kachcha makan ek main
hasraton se ate asman ke tale
jaltibujhti hui kahkashan ek main
mujh ko farigh dinon ki amanat samajh
bhulibisri hui dastan ek main
raunaqen shor mele jhamele tire
apni tanhai ka razdan ek main
ek main apni hi zindagi ka bharam
apni hi maut par nauhakhvan ek main
us taraf sangbari har ik baam se
is taraf ainon ki dukan ek main
vo nahin hai to mohsin ye mat sochna
ab bhatakta phirunga kahan ek main

tire badan se jo chhu kar idhar bhi aata hai
misalerang vo jhonka nazar bhi aata hai
tamam shab jahan jalta hai ik udaas diya
hava ki raah men ik aisa ghar bhi aata hai
vo mujh ko tuut ke chahega chhod jaega
mujhe khabar thi use ye hunar bhi aata hai
ujaad ban men utarta hai ek jugnu bhi
hava ke saath koi hamsafar bhi aata hai
vafa ki kaun si manzil pe us ne chhoda tha
ki vo to yaad hamen bhuul kar bhi aata hai
jahan lahu ke samundar ki had thaharti hai
vahin jaziraelaloguhar bhi aata hai
chale jo zikr farishton ki parsai ka
to zerebahs maqamebashar bhi aata hai
abhi sinan ko sambhale rahen adu mere
ki un safon men kahin mera sar bhi aata hai
kabhi kabhi mujhe milne bulandiyon se koi
shuaesubh ki surat utar bhi aata hai
isi liye main kisi shab na so saka mohsin
vo mahtab kabhi baam par bhi aata hai

ujad ujad ke sanvarti hai tere hijr ki shaam
na puchh kaise guzarti hai tere hijr ki shaam
ye barg barg udasi bikhar rahi hai miri
ki shakh shakh utarti hai tere hijr ki shaam
ujaad ghar men koi chand kab utarta hai
saval mujh se ye karti hai tere hijr ki shaam
mire safar men ik aisa bhi mod aata hai
jab apne aap se darti hai tere hijr ki shaam
bahut aziiz hain dil ko ye zakhm zakhm ruten
inhi ruton men nikharti hai tere hijr ki shaam
ye mera dil ye sarasar nigarkhanaegham
sada isi men utarti hai tere hijr ki shaam
jahan jahan bhi milen teri qurbaton ke nishan
vahan vahan se ubharti hai tere hijr ki shaam
ye hadisa tujhe shayad udaas kar dega
ki mere saath hi marti hai tere hijr ki shaam

ujde hue logon se gurezan na hua kar
halat ki qabron ke ye katbe bhi padha kar
kya janiye kyuun tez hava soch men gum hai
khvabida parindon ko darakhton se uda kar
us shakhs ke tum se bhi marasim hain to honge
vo jhuut na bolega mire samne aa kar
har vaqt ka hansna tujhe barbad na kar de
tanhai ke lamhon men kabhi ro bhi liya kar
vo aaj bhi sadiyon ki masafat pe khada hai
dhunda tha jise vaqt ki divar gira kar
ai dil tujhe dushman ki bhi pahchan kahan hai
tu halqaeyaran men bhi mohtat raha kar
is shab ke muqaddar men sahar hi nahin mohsin
dekha hai kai baar charaghon ko bujha kar

vo dilavar jo siyah shab ke shikari nikle
vo bhi chadhte hue suraj ke pujari nikle
sab ke honton pe mire baad hain baten meri
mere dushman mire lafzon ke bhikari nikle
ik janaza utha maqtal men ajab shaan ke saath
jaise saj kar kisi fateh ki savari nikle
ham ko har daur ki gardish ne salami di hai
ham vo patthar hain jo har daur men bhari nikle
aks koi ho khadokhal tumhare dekhun
bazm koi ho magar baat tumhari nikle
apne dushman se main bevajh khafa tha mohsin
mere qatil to mire apne havari nikle

ye dil ye pagal dil mira kyuun bujh gaya avargi
is dasht men ik shahr tha vo kya hua avargi
kal shab mujhe beshakl ki avaz ne chaunka diya
main ne kaha tu kaun hai us ne kaha avargi
logo bhala is shahr men kaise jiyenge ham jahan
ho jurm tanha sochna lekin saza avargi
ye dard ki tanhaiyan ye dasht ka viran safar
ham log to ukta gae apni suna avargi
ik ajnabi jhonke ne jab puchha mire gham ka sabab
sahra ki bhigi ret par main ne likha avargi
us samt vahshi khvahishon ki zad men paimanevafa
us samt lahron ki dhamak kachcha ghada avargi
kal raat tanha chand ko dekha tha main ne khvab men
mohsin mujhe raas aaegi shayad sada avargi

ye kah gae hain musafir lute gharon vaale
daren hava se parinde khule paron vaale
ye mere dil ki havas dashtebekaran jaisi
vo teri aankh ke tevar samundaron vaale
hava ke haath men kaase hain zard patton ke
kahan gae vo sakhi sabz chadaron vaale
kahan milenge vo agle dinon ke shahzade
pahan ke tan pe libade gadagaron vaale
pahadiyon men ghire ye bujhe bujhe raste
kabhi idhar se guzarte the lashkaron vaale
unhi pe ho kabhi nazil azaab aag ajal
vahi nagar kabhi thahren payambaron vaale

kisi ko dekh ke chup chup se kyuun hue mohsin
kahan gae vo irade sukhanvaron vaale

zaban rakhta huun lekin chup khada huun
main avazon ke ban men ghir gaya huun
mire ghar ka daricha puchhta hai
main saara din kahan phirta raha huun
mujhe mere siva sab log samjhen
main apne aap se kam bolta huun
sitaron se hasad ki intiha hai
main qabron par charaghan kar raha huun
sambhal kar ab havaon se ulajhna
main tujh se peshtar bujhne laga huun
miri qurbat se kyuun khaif hai duniya
samundar huun main khud men gunjta huun
mujhe kab tak sametega vo mohsin
main andar se bahut tuuta hua huun

zakhm ke phuul se taskin talab karti hai
baaz auqat miri ruuh ghazab karti hai
jo tiri zulf se utre hon mire angan men
chandni aise andheron ka adab karti hai
apne insaf ki zanjir na dekho ki yahan
muflisi zehn ki fariyad bhi kab karti hai

har kali matamesadjashnetarab karti hai
sirf din dhalne pe mauquf nahin hai mohsin
zindagi zulf ke saae men bhi shab karti hai

zikreshabefiraq se vahshat use bhi thi
meri tarah kisi se mohabbat use bhi thi
mujh ko bhi shauq tha nae chehron ki diid ka
rasta badal ke chalne ki aadat use bhi thi
is raat der tak vo raha mahveguftugu
masruf main bhi kam tha faraghat use bhi thi
mujh se bichhad ke shahr men ghulmil gaya vo shakhs
halanki shahrbhar se adavat use bhi thi
vo mujh se badh ke zabt ka aadi tha ji gaya
varna har ek saans qayamat use bhi thi
sunta tha vo bhi sab se purani kahaniyan
shayad rafaqaton ki zarurat use bhi thi
tanha hua safar men to mujh pe khula ye bhed
saae se pyaar dhuup se nafrat use bhi thi
mohsin main us se kah na saka yuun bhi haal dil
darpesh ek taaza musibat use bhi thi

aae hain mir kafir ho kar khuda ke ghar men
peshani par hai qashqa zunnar hai kamar men
nazuk badan hai kitna vo shokhchashm dilbar
jaan us ke tan ke aage aati nahin nazar men
siine men tiir us ke tuute hain benihayat
surakh pad gae hain saare mire jigar men
ainda shaam ko ham roya kudha karenge
mutlaq asar na dekha nalidanesahar men
besudh pada rahun huun us mastenaz bin main
aata hai hosh mujh ko ab to pahr pahr men
sirat se guftugu hai kya motabar hai surat
hai ek sukhi lakdi jo bu na ho agar men
hamsayaemughan men muddat se huun chunanche
ik shirakhane ki hai divar mere ghar men
ab subh o shaam shayad girye pe rang aave
rahta hai kuchh jhamakta khunab chashmetar men
aalam men abogil ke kyunkar nibah hoga
asbab gir pada hai saara mira safar men

ashk ankhon men kab nahin aata
lohu aata hai jab nahin aata
hosh jaata nahin raha lekin
jab vo aata hai tab nahin aata
sabr tha ek monisehijran
so vo muddat se ab nahin aata
dil se rukhsat hui koi khvahish
girya kuchh besabab nahin aata

baat ka kis ko dhab nahin aata
ji men kya kya hai apne ai hamdam
par sukhan tabalab nahin aata
duur baitha ghubaremir us se
ishq bin ye adab nahin aata

arsh par barchhiyan chalati hai

baare duniya men raho ghamzada ya shaad raho
aisa kuchh kar ke chalo yaan ki bahut yaad raho
ishqpeche ki tarah husnegiraftari hai
lutf kya sarv ki manind gar azad raho
ham ko divangi shahron hi men khush aati hai
dasht men qais raho koh men farhad raho
vo garan khvab jo hai naaz ka apne so hai
daad bedad raho shab ko ki fariyad raho
mir ham mil ke bahut khush hue tum se pyare
is kharabe men miri jaan tum abad raho

aa jaaen ham nazar jo koi dam bahut hai yaan
mohlat hamen bisanesharar kam bahut hai yaan
yak lahza sinakubi se fursat hamen nahin
yaani ki dil ke jaane ka matam bahut hai yaan
hasil hai kya sivae tarai ke dahr men
uth asman tale se ki shabnam bahut hai yaan
mailbaghair hona tujh abru ka aib hai
thi zor ye kaman vale khamcham bahut hai yaan

vaisa chaman se saada nikalta nahin koi
rangini ek aur khamocham bahut hai yaan
ejazeisvi se nahin bahas ishq men

aine ko utha ki zamin nam bahut hai yaan
shayad ki kaam subh tak apna khinche na mir
ahval aaj shaam se darham bahut hai yaan

aam hukmesharab karta huun
mohtasib ko kabab karta huun
tuk to rah ai binaehasti tu
tujh ko kaisa kharab karta huun
bahs karta huun ho ke abjadkhvan
kis qadar behisab karta huun
koi bujhti hai ye bhadak men abas
tishnagi par itaab karta huun
sar talak abetegh men huun gharq
ab taiin aab aab karta huun
ji men phirta hai mir vo mere
jagta huun ki khvab karta huun

barha goredil jhanka laaya
ab ke shartevafa baja laaya
qadr rakhti na thi mataedil
saare aalam men main dikha laaya
dil ki yak qatra khuun nahin hai besh
ek aalam ke sar bala laaya
sab pe jis baar ne girani ki
us ko ye natavan utha laaya
dil mujhe us gali men le ja kar
aur bhi khaak men mila laaya
ibtida hi men mar gae sab yaar
ishq ki kaun intiha laaya
ab to jaate hain butkade se mir
phir milenge agar khuda laaya

aao kabhu to paas hamare bhi naaz se
karna suluk khuub hai ahleniyaz se
phirte ho kya darakhton ke saae men duur duur
kar lo muvafaqat kisu bebargosaz se
hijran men us ke zindagi karna bhala na tha
kotahi jo na hove ye umredaraz se
manindesubha uqde na dil ke kabhu khule
ji apna kyuun ki uchte na roze namaz se
karta hai chhed chhed hamara jigar tamam
vo dekhna tira mizhaenimbaz se
dil par ho ikhtiyar to hargiz na kariye ishq
parhez kariye is marazejangudaz se
aage bichha ke nata ko laate the tegh o tasht
karte the yaani khuun to ik imtiyaz se
maane hon kyuun ki giryaekhunin ke ishq men
hai rabtekhas chashm ko ifshaeraz se
shayad sharabkhane men shab ko rahe the mir
khele tha ek mughbacha mohrenamaz se

baten hamari yaad rahen phir baten aisi na suniyega
padhte kisu ko suniyega to der talak sar dhuniyega
sai o talash bahut si rahegi is andaz ke kahne ki
sohbat men ulma fuzla ki ja kar padhiye ginyega
dil ki tasalli jab ki hogi guft o shunud se logon ki
aag phunkegi gham ki badan men us men jaliye bhuniyega
garm ashar mir daruna daghon se ye bhar denge
zardru shahr men phiriyega galiyon men ne gul chuniyega

arzuen hazar rakhte hain
to bhi ham dil ko maar rakhte hain
barq kamhausla hai ham bhi to
dil ko beqarar rakhte hain
ghair hi maurideinayat hai
ham bhi to tum se pyaar rakhte hain
na nigah ne payam ne vaada
naam ko ham bhi yaar rakhte hain
ham se khushzamzama kahan yuun to
lab o lahja hazar rakhte hain
chotte dil ke hain butan mashhur
bas yahi etibar rakhte hain
phir bhi karte hain mir sahab ishq
hain javan ikhtiyar rakhte hain

ab jo ik hasratejavani hai
umrerafta ki ye nishani hai
rashkeyusuf hai aah vaqteaziz
umr ik barekarvani hai
girya har vaqt ka nahin behech
dil men koi ghamenihani hai
ham qafaszad qaidi hain varna
ta chaman ek parfishani hai
us ki shamshir tez hai hamdam
mar rahenge jo zindagani hai
ghamoranjoalam niko yaan se
sab tumhari hi mehrbani hai
khaak thi maujzan jahan men aur
ham ko dhoka ye tha ki paani hai
yaan hue mir tum barabar khaak
vaan vahi naaz o sargirani hai

bani thi kuchh ik us se muddat ke baad
so phir bigdi pahli hi sohbat ke baad
judai ke halat main kya kahun
qayamat thi ek ek saaat ke baad
mua kohkan besutun khod kar
ye rahat hui aisi mehnat ke baad
laga aag paani ko daude hai tu
ye garmi tiri is shararat ke baad
kahe ko hamare kab un ne suna
koi baat maani so minnat ke baad
sukhan ki na taklif ham se karo
lahu tapke hai ab shikayat ke baad
nazar mir ne kaisi hasrat se ki
bahut roe ham us ki rukhsat ke baad

barangebuegul us baagh ke ham ashna hote
ki hamrahesaba tuk sair karte phir hava hote
sarapa aarzu hone ne banda kar diya ham ko
vagarna ham khuda the gar dilebemuddaa hote
falak ai kaash ham ko khaak hi rakhta ki is men ham
ghubarerah hote ya kasu ki khakepa hote
ilahi kaise hote hain jinhen hai bandagi khvahish
hamen to sharm damangir hoti hai khuda hote
tu hai kis nahiye se ai dayareishq kya janun
tire bashindagan ham kaash saare bevafa hote
ab aise hain ki sanea ke mizaj uupar baham pahunche
jo khatirkhvah apne ham hue hote to kya hote
kahin jo kuchh malamat gar baja hai mir kya janen
unhen maalum tab hota ki vaise se juda hote

chalte ho to chaman ko chaliye kahte hain ki baharan hai
paat hare hain phuul khile hain kamkam badobaran hai
rang hava se yuun tapke hai jaise sharab chuvate hain
aage ho maikhane ke niklo ahdebadagusaran hai
ishq ke maidandaron men bhi marne ka hai vasf bahut
yaani musibat aisi uthana karekarguzaran hai
dil hai daagh jigar hai tukde aansu saare khuun hue
lohu paani ek kare ye ishqelalaazaran hai
kohkan o majnun ki khatir dashtokoh men ham na gae
ishq men ham ko mir nihayat paseizzatdaran hai

chaman men gul ne jo kal davaejamal kiya
jamaleyar ne munh us ka khuub laal kiya
falak ne aah tiri rah men ham ko paida kar
barangesabzaenurasta paemal kiya
rahi thi dam ki kashakash gale men kuchh baaqi
so us ki tegh ne jhagda hi infisal kiya
miri ab ankhen nahin khultin zoaf se hamdam
na kah ki niind men hai tu ye kya khayal kiya
baharerafta phir aai tire tamashe ko
chaman ko yumneqadam ne tire nihal kiya
javabnama siyahi ka apni hai vo zulf
kisu ne hashr ko ham se agar saval kiya
laga na dil ko kahin kya suna nahin tu ne
jo kuchh ki mir ka is ashiqi ne haal kiya

dekh to dil ki jaan se uthta hai
ye dhuan sa kahan se uthta hai
gor kis diljale ki hai ye falak
shola ik subh yaan se uthta hai
khanaedil se zinhar na ja
koi aise makan se uthta hai
naala sar khinchta hai jab mera
shor ik asman se uthta hai
ladti hai us ki chashmeshokh jahan
ek ashob vaan se uthta hai
sudh le ghar ki bhi sholaeavaz
duud kuchh ashiyan se uthta hai
baithne kaun de hai phir us ko
jo tire astan se uthta hai
yuun uthe aah us gali se ham
jaise koi jahan se uthta hai
ishq ik mir bhari patthar hai
kab ye tujh natavan se uthta hai

faqirana aae sada kar chale
ki myaan khush raho ham dua kar chale
jo tujh bin na jiine ko kahte the ham
so is ahd ko ab vafa kar chale
shifa apni taqdir hi men na thi
ki maqdur tak to dava kar chale
pade aise asbab payanekar
ki nachar yuun ji jala kar chale
vo kya chiiz hai aah jis ke liye
har ik chiiz se dil utha kar chale
koi naumidana karte nigah
so tum ham se munh bhi chhupa kar chale
bahut aarzu thi gali ki tiri
so yaan se lahu men naha kar chale
dikhai diye yuun ki bekhud kiya
hamen aap se bhi juda kar chale
jabin sajda karte hi karte gai
haqebandagi ham ada kar chale
parastish ki yaan tak ki ai but tujhe
nazar men sabhon ki khuda kar chale
jhade phuul jis rang gulbun se yuun
chaman men jahan ke ham aa kar chale
na dekha ghamedostan shukr hai
hamin daagh apna dikha kar chale
gai umr darbandefikreghazal
so is fan ko aisa bada kar chale
kahen kya jo puchhe koi ham se mir
jahan men tum aae the kya kar chale

gham raha jab tak ki dam men dam raha
dil ke jaane ka nihayat gham raha
husn tha tera bahut alamfareb
khat ke aane par bhi ik aalam raha
dil na pahuncha goshaedaman talak
qatraekhun tha mizha par jam raha
sunte hain laila ke kheme ko siyah
us men majnun ka magar matam raha
jamaeehramezahid par na ja
tha haram men lek namahram raha
zulfen kholin to tu tuk aaya nazar
umr bhar yaan kamedil barham raha
us ke lab se talkh ham sunte rahe
apne haq men abehaivan sam raha
mere rone ki haqiqat jis men thi
ek muddat tak vo kaghaz nam raha
subhepiri shaam hone aai mir
tu na cheta yaan bahut din kam raha

ham aap hi ko apna maqsud jante hain
apne sivae kis ko maujud jante hain
ijzoniyaz apna apni taraf hai saara
is mushtekhak ko ham masjud jante hain
suratpazir ham bin hargiz nahin ve maane
ahlenazar hamin ko maabud jante hain
ishq un ki aql ko hai jo masiva hamare
nachiz jante hain nabud jante hain
apni hi sair karne ham jalvagar hue the
is ramz ko valekin madud jante hain
yarab kase hai naaqa har ghuncha is chaman ka
rahevafa ko ham to masdud jante hain
ye zulmebenihayat dushvartar ki khuban
badvaziyon ko apni mahmud jante hain
kya jaane daab sohbat az khvesh raftagan ka
majlis men shaikhsahib kuchh kuud jante hain
mar kar bhi haath aave to mir muft hai vo
ji ke ziyan ko bhi ham suud jante hain

hamare aage tira jab kisu ne naam liya
dilesitamzada ko ham ne thaam thaam liya
qasam jo khaiye to talaezulekha ki
azizemisr ka bhi sahab ik ghulam liya
kharab rahte the masjid ke aage maikhane
nigahemast ne saaqi ki intiqam liya
vo kajravish na mila raste men mujh se kabhi
na sidhi tarah se un ne mira salam liya
maza dikhavenge berahmi ka tiri sayyad
gar iztirabeasiri ne zeredam liya
mire saliqe se meri nibhi mohabbat men
tamam umr main nakamiyon se kaam liya
agarche goshaguzin huun main shairon men mir
pa mere shor ne ruezamin tamam liya

hasti apni habab ki si hai
ye numaish sarab ki si hai
nazuki us ke lab ki kya kahiye
pankhudi ik gulab ki si hai
chashmedil khol is bhi aalam par
yaan ki auqat khvab ki si hai
baar baar us ke dar pe jaata huun
halat ab iztirab ki si hai
nuqtaekhal se tira abru
bait ik intikhab ki si hai
main jo bola kaha ki ye avaz
usi khanakharab ki si hai
atishegham men dil bhuna shayad
der se bu kabab ki si hai
dekhiye abr ki tarah ab ke
meri chashmepurab ki si hai
mir un nimbaz ankhon men
saari masti sharab ki si hai

is ahd men ilahi mohabbat ko kya hua
chhoda vafa ko un ne muravvat ko kya hua
ummidvarevadaedidar mar chale
aate hi aate yaaro qayamat ko kya hua
kab tak tazallum aah bhala marg ke taiin
kuchh pesh aaya vaqia rahmat ko kya hua
us ke gae par aise gae dil se hamnashin
malum bhi hua na ki taqat ko kya hua
bakhshish ne mujh ko abrekaram ki kiya khajil
ai chashm josheashkenadamat ko kya hua
jaata hai yaar teghbakaf ghair ki taraf
ai kushtaesitam tiri ghairat ko kya hua
thi sabeashiqi ki badayat hi mir par
kya janiye ki halenihayat ko kya hua

ishq hamare khayal pada hai khvab gai aram gaya
ji ka jaana thahar raha hai subh gaya ya shaam gaya
ishq kiya so diin gaya iman gaya islam gaya
dil ne aisa kaam kiya kuchh jis se main nakam gaya
kis kis apni kal ko rove hijran men bekal us ka
khvab gai hai taab gai hai chain gaya aram gaya
aaya yaan se jaana hi to ji ka chhupana kya hasil
aaj gaya ya kal javega subh gaya ya shaam gaya
haae javani kya kya kahiye shor saron men rakhte the
ab kya hai vo ahd gaya vo mausam vo hangam gaya
gaali jhidki khashmokhushunat ye to saredast aksar hain
lutf gaya ehsan gaya inaam gaya ikram gaya
likhna kahna tark hua tha aapas men to muddat se
ab jo qarar kiya hai dil se khat bhi gaya paigham gaya
nalaemir savad men ham tak doshin shab se nahin aaya
shayad shahr se us zalim ke ashiq vo badnam gaya

ishq men zillat hui khiffat hui tohmat hui
akhir akhir jaan di yaron ne ye sohbat hui
aks us bedid ka to muttasil padta tha subh
din chadhe kya janun aine ki kya surat hui
lauhesina par miri sau nezaekhatti lage
khastagi is dilshikasta ki isi babat hui
kholte hi ankhen phir yaan mundni ham ko padin
diid kya koi kare vo kis qadar mohlat hui
paanv mera kalbaeahzan men ab rahta nahin
rafta rafta us taraf jaane ki mujh ko lat hui
mar gaya avara ho kar main to jaise gardbad
par jise ye vaqia pahuncha use vahshat hui
shaad o khushtale koi hoga kisu ko chaah kar
main to kulfat men raha jab se mujhe ulfat hui
dil ka jaana aaj kal taaza hua ho to kahun
guzre us bhi sanehe ko hamnashin muddat hui
shauqedil ham natavanon ka likha jaata hai kab
ab talak aap hi pahunchne ki agar taqat hui
kya kafedast ek maidan tha bayaban ishq ka
jaan se jab us men guzre tab hamen rahat hui
yuun to ham ajiztarinekhalqealam hain vale
dekhiyo qudrat khuda ki gar hamen qudrat hui
gosh zad chatpat hi marna ishq men apne hua
kis ko is bimariejankah se fursat hui
bezaban jo kahte hain mujh ko so chup rah jaenge
marke men hashr ke gar baat ki rukhsat hui
ham na kahte the ki naqsh us ka nahin naqqash sahl
chand saara lag gaya tab nimrukh surat hui
is ghazal par shaam se to sufiyon ko vajd tha
phir nahin malum kuchh majlis ki kya halat hui
kam kisu ko mir ki mayyat ki haath aai namaz
naash par us besaropa ki bala kasrat hui

jab naam tira lijiye tab chashm bhar aave
is zindagi karne ko kahan se jigar aave
talvar ka bhi maara khuda rakkhe hai zalim
ye to ho koi goreghariban men dar aave
maikhana vo manzar hai ki har subh jahan shaikh
divar pe khurshid ka masti se sar aave
kya janen ve murghanegiraftarechaman ko
jin tak ki basadnaz nasimesahar aave
tu subh qadamranja kare tuk to hai varna
kis vaste ashiq ki shabegham basar aave
har su saretaslim rakhe saideharam hain
vo saidfagan teghbakaf ta kidhar aave
divaron se sar marte phirne ka gaya vaqt
ab tu hi magar aap kabhu dar se dar aave
vaaiz nahin kaifiyyatemaikhana se agah
yak jura badal varna ye mindil dhar aave
sannaa hain sab khvar azaan jumla huun main bhi
hai aib bada us men jise kuchh hunar aave
ai vo ki tu baitha hai sarerah pe zinhar
kahiyo jo kabhu mir balakash idhar aave
mat dashtemohabbat men qadam rakh ki khizar ko
har gaam pe is rah men safar se hazar aave

jab rone baithta huun tab kya kasar rahe hai
rumal do do din tak juun abr tar rahe hai
ahesahar ki meri barchhi ke vasvase se
khurshid ke munh uupar aksar sipar rahe hai
aagah to rahiye us ki tarzerahoravish se
aane men us ke lekin kis ko khabar rahe hai
un rozon itni ghaflat achchhi nahin idhar se
ab iztirab ham ko do do pahr rahe hai
abehayat ki si saari ravish hai us ki
par jab vo uth chale hai ek aadh mar rahe hai
talvar ab laga hai bedol paas rakhne
khuun aaj kal kisu ka vo shokh kar rahe hai
dar se kabhu jo aate dekha hai main ne us ko
tab se udhar hi aksar meri nazar rahe hai
akhir kahan talak ham ik roz ho chukenge
barson se vaadaeshab har subh par rahe hai
mir ab bahar aai sahra men chal junun kar
koi bhi faslegul men nadan ghar rahe hai

jiteji kuchaedildar se jaaya na gaya
us ki divar ka sar se mire saaya na gaya
kavkave mizhaeyar o dilezaronazar
guth gae aise shitabi ki chhudaya na gaya
vo to kal der talak dekhta idhar ko raha
ham se hi haletabah apna dikhaya na gaya
garmrau rahefana ka nahin ho sakta patang
us se to shamanamat sar bhi kataya na gaya
pasenamusemohabbat tha ki farhad ke paas
besutun samne se apne uthaya na gaya
khaak tak kuchaedildar ki chhani ham ne
justuju ki pe dilegumshuda paaya na gaya
atishetez judai men yakayak us bin
dil jala yuun ki tanik ji bhi jalaya na gaya
mah ne aa samne shab yaad dilaya tha use
phir vo ta subh mire ji se bhulaya na gaya
zereshamshiresitam mir tadapna kaisa
sar bhi taslimemohabbat men hilaya na gaya
ji men aata hai ki kuchh aur bhi mauzun kiije
dardedil ek ghazal men to sunaya na gaya

jin jin ko tha ye ishq ka azar mar gae
aksar hamare saath ke bimar mar gae
hota nahin hai us labenaukhat pe koi sabz
iisa o khizr kya sabhi yakbar mar gae
yuun kanonkan gul ne na jaana chaman men aah
sar ko patak ke ham pasedivar mar gae
sad karvan vafa hai koi puchhta nahin
goya mataedil ke kharidar mar gae
majnun na dasht men hai na farhad koh men
tha jin se lutfezindagi ve yaar mar gae
gar zindagi yahi hai jo karte hain ham asiir
to ve hi ji gae jo giraftar mar gae
afsos ve shahid ki jo qatlgah men
lagte hi us ke haath ki talvar mar gae
tujh se dochar hone ki hasrat ke mubtila
jab ji hue vabal to nachar mar gae
ghabra na mir ishq men us sahalezist par
jab bas chala na kuchh to mire yaar mar gae

jin ke liye apne to yuun jaan nikalte hain
is raah men ve jaise anjan nikalte hain
kya tiresitam us ke siine men bhi tuute the
jis zakhm ko chirun huun paikan nikalte hain
mat sahl hamen jaano phirta hai falak barson
tab khaak ke parde se insan nikalte hain
kis ka hai qimash aisa gudad bhare hain saare
dekho na jo logon ke divan nikalte hain
gah lohu tapakta hai gah lakhtedil ankhon se
ya tukde jigar hi ke har aan nikalte hain
kariye to gila kis se jaisi thi hamen khvahish
ab vaise hi ye apne arman nikalte hain
jagah se bhi jaate ho munh se bhi khashin ho kar
ve harf nahin hain jo shayan nikalte hain
so kaahe ko apni tu jogi ki si pheri hai
barson men kabhu idhar ham aan nikalte hain
un ainaruyon ke kya mir bhi ashiq hain
jab ghar se nikalte hain hairan nikalte hain

jis sar ko ghurur aaj hai yaan tajvari ka
kal us pe yahin shor hai phir nauhagari ka
sharminda tire rukh se hai rukhsar pari ka
chalta nahin kuchh aage tire kabkedari ka
afaq ki manzil se gaya kaun salamat
asbab luta raah men yaan har safari ka
zindan men bhi shorish na gai apne junun ki
ab sang mudava hai is ashuftasari ka
har zakhmejigar davaremahshar se hamara
insaftalab hai tiri bedadgari ka
apni to jahan aankh ladi phir vahin dekho
aine ko lapka hai pareshannazari ka
sad mausamegul ham ko tahebal hi guzre
maqdur na dekha kabhu bebalopari ka
is rang se jhamke hai palak par ki kahe tu
tukda hai mira ashk aqiqejigari ka
kal sair kiya ham ne samundar ko bhi ja kar
tha dastenigar panjaemizhgan ki tari ka
le saans bhi ahista ki nazuk hai bahut kaam
afaq ki is kargaheshishagari ka
tuk mirejigarsokhta ki jald khabar le
kya yaar bharosa hai charaghesahari ka

jo is shor se mir rota rahega
to hamsaya kaahe ko sota rahega
main vo rone vaala jahan se chala huun
jise abr har saal rota rahega
mujhe kaam rone se aksar hai naseh
tu kab tak mire munh ko dhota rahega
bas ai girya ankhen tiri kya nahin hain
kahan tak jahan ko dubota rahega
mire dil ne vo naala paida kiya hai
jaras ke bhi jo hosh khota rahega
tu yuun galiyan ghair ko shauq se de
hamen kuchh kahega to hota rahega
bas ai mir mizhgan se ponchh ansuon ko
tu kab tak ye moti pirota rahega

kuchh maujehava pechan ai mir nazar aai
shayad ki bahar aai zanjir nazar aai
dilli ke na the kuche auraqemusavvar the
jo shakl nazar aai tasvir nazar aai
maghrur bahut the ham aansu ki sarayat par
so subh ke hone ko tasir nazar aai
gulbar kare haiga asbabesafar shayad
ghunche ki tarah bulbul dilgir nazar aai
us ki to dilazari behech hi thi yaaro
kuchh tum ko hamari bhi taqsir nazar aai

kya haqiqat kahun ki kya hai ishq
haqshanason ke haan khuda hai ishq
dil laga ho to ji jahan se utha
maut ka naam pyaar ka hai ishq
aur tadbir ko nahin kuchh dakhl
ishq ke dard ki dava hai ishq
kya dubaya muhit men gham ke
ham ne jaana tha ashna hai ishq
ishq se ja nahin koi khali
dil se le arsh tak bhara hai ishq
kohkan kya pahad katega
parde men zorazma hai ishq
ishq hai ishq karne valon ko
kaisa kaisa baham kiya hai ishq
kaun maqsad ko ishq bin pahuncha
aarzu ishq muddaa hai ishq
mir marna pade hai khuban par
ishq mat kar ki bad bala hai ishq

kya kahun tum se main ki kya hai ishq
jaan ka rog hai bala hai ishq
ishq hi ishq hai jahan dekho
saare aalam men bhar raha hai ishq
ishq hai tarz o taur ishq ke taiin
kahin banda kahin khuda hai ishq
ishq maashuq ishq ashiq hai
yaani apna hi mubtala hai ishq
gar parastish khuda ki sabit ki
kisu surat men ho bhala hai ishq
dilkash aisa kahan hai dushmanejan
muddai hai pa muddaa hai ishq
hai hamare bhi taur ka ashiq
jis kisi ko kahin hua hai ishq
koi khvahan nahin mohabbat ka
tu kahe jinsenarava hai ishq
mirji zard hote jaate ho
kya kahin tum ne bhi kiya hai ishq

lazzat se nahin khali janon ka khapa jaana
kab khizr o masiha ne marne ka maza jaana
ham jahohasham yaan ka kya kahiye ki kya jaana
khatim ko sulaiman ki angushtarepa jaana
ye bhi hai ada koi khurshid namat pyare
munh subh dikha jaana phir shaam chhupa jaana
kab bandagi meri si banda karega koi
jaane hai khuda us ko main tujh ko khuda jaana
tha naaz bahut ham ko danist par apni bhi
akhir vo bura nikla ham jis ko bhala jaana
gardankashi kya hasil manind bagule ki
is dasht men sar gaade juun sail chala jaana
is giryaekhunin ka ho zabt to behtar hai
achchha nahin chehre par lohu ka baha jaana
ye naqsh dilon par se jaane ka nahin us ko
ashiq ke huquq aa kar nahaq bhi mita jaana
dhab dekhne ka idhar aisa hi tumhara tha
jaate to ho par ham se tuk aankh mila jaana
us shama ki majlis men jaana hamen phir vaan se
ik zakhmezaban taaza har roz utha jaana
ai shoreqayamat ham sote hi na rah javen
is raah se nikle to ham ko bhi jaga jaana
kya paani ke mol aa kar malik ne guhar becha
hai sakht giran sasta yusuf ka bika jaana
hai meri tiri nisbat ruuh aur jasad ki si
kab aap se main tujh ko ai jaan juda jaana
jaati hai guzar ji par us vaqt qayamat si
yaad aave hai jab tera yakbargi aa jaana
barson se mire us ki rahti hai yahi sohbat
tegh us ko uthana to sar mujh ko jhuka jaana
kab mir basar aae tum vaise farebi se
dil ko to laga baithe lekin na laga jaana

aage jamaleyar ke maazur ho gaya
gul ik chaman men didaebenur ho gaya
ik chashmemuntazar hai ki dekhe hai kab se raah
jon zakhm teri duuri men nasur ho gaya
qismat to dekh shaikh ko jab lahar aai tab
darvaza shira khane ka maamur ho gaya
pahuncha qarib marg ke vo saidenaqubul
jo teri saidegah se tak duur ho gaya
dekha ye navnosh ki nishefiraq se
siina tamam khanaezambur ho gaya
is mahechardah ka chhape ishq kyunke aah
ab to tamam shahr men mashhur ho gaya
shayad kaso ke dil ko lagi us gali men chot
meri baghal men shishaedil chuur ho gaya
lasha mira tasalli na zerezamin hua
jab tak na aan kar vo saregor ho gaya
dekha jo main ne yaar to vo mir hi nahin
tere ghamefiraq men ranjur ho gaya

rahedureishq men rota hai kya
aage aage dekhiye hota hai kya
qafile men subh ke ik shor hai
yaani ghafil ham chale sota hai kya
sabz hoti hi nahin ye sarzamin
tukhmekhvahish dil men tu bota hai kya
ye nishaneishq hain jaate nahin
daagh chhati ke abas dhota hai kya
ghairateyusuf hai ye vaqteaziz
mir us ko raegan khota hai kya

ahesahar ne sozishedil ko mita diya
us baav ne hamen to diya sa bujha diya
samjhi na baad subh ki aa kar utha diya
is fitnaezamana ko nahaq jaga diya
poshida razeishq chala jaae tha sau aaj
betaqati ne dil ki vo parda utha diya
us maujkhez dahr men ham ko qaza ne aah
paani ke bulbule ki tarah se mita diya
thi laag us ki tegh ko ham se sau ishq ne
donon ko maarke men gale se mila diya
sab shoremaoman ko liye sar men mar gae
yaron ko is fasane ne akhir sula diya
avarganeishq ka puchha jo main nishan
mushteghubar le ke saba ne uda diya
ajza badan ke jitne the paani ho bah gae
akhir gudaz ishq ne ham ko baha diya
kya kuchh na tha azal men na taala jo the durust
ham ko dilshikasta qaza ne dila diya
goya muhasba mujhe dena tha ishq ka
us taur dil si chiiz ko main ne laga diya
muddat rahegi yaad tire chehre ki jhalak
jalve ko jis ne maah ke ji se bhula diya
ham ne to sadgi se kya ji ka bhi ziyan
dil jo diya tha so to diya sar juda diya
boi kabab sokhta aai dimagh men
shayad jigar bhi atishegham ne jila diya
taklif dardedil ki abas hamnashin ne ki
dardesukhan ne mere sabhon ko rula diya
un ne to tegh khinchi thi par ji chala ke mir
ham ne bhi ek dam men tamasha dikha diya

aae hain mir munh ko banae khafa se aaj
shayad bigad gai hai kuchh us bevafa se aaj
vashud hui na dil ko faqiron ke bhi mile
khulti nahin girah ye kasu ki dua se aaj
jiine men ikhtiyar nahin varna hamnashin
ham chahte hain maut to apni khuda se aaj
saaqi tuk ek mausamegul ki taraf bhi dekh
tapka pade hai rang chaman men hava se aaj
tha ji men us se miliye to kya kya na kahiye mir
par kuchh kaha gaya na ghamedil haya se aaj

avegi meri qabr se avaz mere baad
ubhrenge ishqedil se tire raaz mere baad
jiina mira to tujh ko ghanimat hai nasamajh
khinga kaun phir ye tire naaz mere baad
shamemazar aur ye sozejigar mira
har shab karenge zindagi nasaz mere baad
hasrat hai is ke dekhne ki dil men beqayas
aghlab ki meri ankhen rahen baaz mere baad
karta huun main jo naale saranjam baagh men
munh dekho phir karenge ham avaz mere baad
bin gul mua hi main to pa tu ja ke lautiyo
sehnechaman men ai pareparvaz mere baad
baitha huun mir marne ko apne men mustaid
paida na honge mujh se bhi janbaz mere baad

ham hue tum hue ki mir hue
us ki zulfon ke sab asiir hue
jin ki khatir ki ustukhvanshikni
so ham un ke nishanetir hue
nahin aate kaso ki ankhon men
ho ke ashiq bahut haqir hue
aage ye beadaiyan kab thiin
in dinon tum bahut sharir hue
apne rote hi rote sahra ke
goshe goshe men abgir hue
aisi hasti adam men dakhil hai
nai javan ham na tifleshir hue
ek dam thi numud buud apni
ya safedi ki ya akhir hue
yaani manindesubh duniya men
ham jo paida hue sau piir hue
mat mil ahleduval ke ladkon se
mirji un se mil faqir hue

munh taka hi kare hai jis tis ka
hairati hai ye aina kis ka
shaam se kuchh bujha sa rahta huun
dil hua hai charagh muflis ka
the bure mughbachon ke tevar lek
shaikh maikhane se bhala khiska
daagh ankhon se khil rahe hain sab
haath dasta hua hai nargis ka
bahr kamzarf hai basanehabab
kasalais ab hua hai tu jis ka
faiz ai abr chashmetar se utha
aaj daman vasia hai is ka
taab kis ko jo halemir sune
haal hi aur kuchh hai majlis ka

patta patta buuta buuta haal hamara jaane hai
jaane na jaane gul hi na jaane baagh to saara jaane hai
lagne na de bas ho to us ke gauharegosh ko baale tak
us ko falak chashmmahokhur ki putli ka taara jaane hai
aage us mutakabbir ke ham khuda khuda kiya karte hain
kab maujud khuda ko vo maghrurekhudara jaane hai
ashiq sa to saada koi aur na hoga duniya men
ji ke ziyan ko ishq men us ke apna vaara jaane hai
charagari bimariedil ki rasmeshahrehusn nahin
varna dilbarenadan bhi is dard ka chara jaane hai
kya hi shikarfarebi par maghrur hai vo sayyad bacha
taair udte hava men saare apne asara jaane hai
mehr o vafa o lutfoinayat ek se vaqif in men nahin
aur to sab kuchh tanz o kinaya ramz o ishara jaane hai
kya kya fitne sar par us ke laata hai mashuq apna
jis bedil betabotavan ko ishq ka maara jaane hai
rakhnon se divarechaman ke munh ko le hai chhupa yaani
in surakhon ke tuk rahne ko sau ka nazara jaane hai
tishnaekhun hai apna kitna mir bhi nadan talkhikash
dumdar abetegh ko us ke abegavara jaane hai

sher ke parde men main ne gham sunaya hai bahut
marsiye ne dil ke mere bhi rulaya hai bahut
besabab aata nahin ab dambadam ashiq ko ghash
dard khincha hai nihayat ranj uthaya hai bahut
vaadi o kohsar men rota huun dadhen maar maar
dilbaraneshahr ne mujh ko sataya hai bahut
va nahin hota kisu se dil girafta ishq ka
zahiran ghamgin use rahna khush aaya hai bahut
mir gumgashta ka milna ittifaqi amr hai
jab kabhu paaya hai khvahishmand paaya hai bahut

tha mustaar husn se us ke jo nuur tha
khurshid men bhi us hi ka zarra zuhur tha
hangama garmkun jo dilenasubur tha
paida har ek naale se shorenushur tha
pahuncha jo aap ko to main pahuncha khuda ke taiin
malum ab hua ki bahut main bhi duur tha
atish buland dil ki na thi varna ai kalim
yak shoala barqekhiramanesadkohetur tha
majlis men raat ek tire partave baghair
kya shama kya patang har ik behuzur tha
us fasl men ki gul ka gareban bhi hai hava
divana ho gaya so bahut zishuur tha
munim ke paas qaqum o sanjab tha to kya
us rind ki bhi raat guzar gai jo uur tha
ham khaak men mile to mile lekin ai siphar
us shokh ko bhi raah pe laana zarur tha
kal paanv ek kasaesar par jo aa gaya
yaksar vo ustukhvan shikaston se chuur tha
kahne laga ki dekh ke chal raah bekhabar
main bhi kabhu kisu ka sarepurghurur tha
tha vo to rashkehurebahishti hamin men mir
samjhe na ham to fahm ka apni qusur tha

ulti ho gaiin sab tadbiren kuchh na dava ne kaam kiya
dekha is bimariedil ne akhir kaam tamam kiya
ahdejavani ro ro kaata piiri men liin ankhen muund
yaani raat bahut the jaage subh hui aram kiya
harf nahin janbakhshi men us ki khubi apni qismat ki
ham se jo pahle kah bheja so marne ka paigham kiya
nahaq ham majburon par ye tohmat hai mukhtari ki
chahte hain so aap karen hain ham ko abas badnam kiya
saare rind aubash jahan ke tujh se sujud men rahte hain
banke tedhe tirchhe tikhe sab ka tujh ko imaam kiya
sarzad ham se beadabi to vahshat men bhi kam hi hui
koson us ki or gae par sajda har har gaam kiya
kis ka kaaba kaisa qibla kaun haram hai kya ehram
kuche ke us ke bashindon ne sab ko yahin se salam kiya
shaikh jo hai masjid men nanga raat ko tha maikhane men
jubba khirqa kurta topi masti men inaam kiya
kaash ab burqa munh se utha de varna phir kya hasil hai
aankh munde par un ne go didar ko apne aam kiya
yaan ke sapid o siyah men ham ko dakhl jo hai so itna hai
raat ko ro ro subh kiya ya din ko juun tuun shaam kiya
subh chaman men us ko kahin taklifehava le aai thi
rukh se gul ko mol liya qamat se sarv ghulam kiya
saadesimin donon us ke haath men la kar chhod diye
bhule us ke qauloqasam par haae khayalekham kiya
kaam hue hain saare zaaea har saaat ki samajat se
istighna ki chauguni un ne juun juun main ibram kiya
aise ahueramkhurda ki vahshat khoni mushkil thi
sehr kiya eajaz kiya jin logon ne tujh ko raam kiya
mir ke dinomazhab ko ab puchhte kya ho un ne to
qashqa khincha dair men baitha kab ka tark islam kiya

umr bhar ham rahe sharabi se
dilepurkhun ki ik gulabi se
ji dhaha jaae hai sahar se aah
raat guzregi kis kharabi se
khilna kam kam kali ne sikha hai
us ki ankhon ki nimkhvabi se
burqa uthte hi chand sa nikla
daagh huun us ki behijabi se
kaam the ishq men bahut par mir
ham hi farigh hue shitabi se

us ka khayal chashm se shab khvab le gaya
qasme ki ishq ji se mire taab le gaya
kin nindon ab tu soti hai ai chashmegiryanak
mizhgan to khol shahr ko sailab le gaya
aave jo mastaba men to sun lo ki raah se
vaaiz ko ek jamemaienab le gaya
ne dil raha baja hai na sabr o havas o hosh
aaya jo saileishq sab asbab le gaya
mere huzur shama ne girya jo sar kiya
roya main is qadar ki mujhe aab le gaya
ahval us shikar zubun ka hai jaae rahm
jis natavan ko muft na qassab le gaya
munh ki jhalak se yaar ke behosh ho gae
shab ham ko mir partavemahtab le gaya

yaaro mujhe muaaf rakho main nashe men huun
ab do to jaam khali hi do main nashe men huun
ek ek qurt daur men yuun hi mujhe bhi do
jamesharab pur na karo main nashe men huun
masti se darhami hai miri guftugu ke biich
jo chaho tum bhi mujh ko kaho main nashe men huun
ya hathon haath lo mujhe manindejamemai
ya thodi duur saath chalo main nashe men huun
maazur huun jo paanv mira betarah pade
tum sargiran to mujh se na ho main nashe men huun
bhagi namazejuma to jaati nahin hai kuchh
chalta huun main bhi tuk to raho main nashe men huun
nazukmizaj aap qayamat hain mir ji
juun shisha mere munh na lago main nashe men huun

zakhm jhele daagh bhi khaae bahut
dil laga kar ham to pachhtae bahut
jab na tab jagah se tum jaaya kiye
ham to apni or se aae bahut
dair se sueharam aaya na tuk
ham mizaj apna idhar laae bahut
phuul gul shams o qamar saare hi the
par hamen in men tumhin bhaae bahut
gar buka is shor se shab ko hai to
rovenge sone ko hamsae bahut
vo jo nikla subh jaise aftab
rashk se gul phuul murjhae bahut
mir se puchha jo main ashiq ho tum
ho ke kuchh chupke se sharmae bahut

aae kya kya yaad nazar jab padti in dalanon par
us ka kaghaz chipka dena ghar ke raushandanon par
aaj bhi jaise shane par tum haath mire rakh deti ho
chalte chalte ruk jaata huun saari ki dukanon par
barkha ki to baat hi chhodo chanchal hai purvai bhi
jaane kis ka sabz dupatta phenk gai hai dhanon par
shahr ke tapte futpathon par gaanv ke mausam saath chalen
budhe bargad haath sa rakh den mere jalte shanon par
saste damon le to aate lekin dil tha bhar aaya
jaane kis ka naam khuda tha pital ke guldanon par
us ka kya manbhed bataun us ka kya andaz kahun
baat bhi meri sunna chahe haath bhi rakkhe kanon par
aur bhi siina kasne lagta aur kamar bal kha jaati
jab bhi us ke paanv phisalne lagte the dhalvanon par
sher to un par likkhe lekin auron se mansub kiye
un ko kya kya ghussa aaya nazmon ke unvanon par
yaaro apne ishq ke qisse yuun bhi kam mashhur nahin
kal to shayad novel likkhe jaaen in rumanon par

ashar mire yuun to zamane ke liye hain
kuchh sher faqat un ko sunane ke liye hain
ab ye bhi nahin thiik ki har dard mita den
kuchh dard kaleje se lagane ke liye hain
socho to badi chiiz hai tahzib badan ki
varna ye faqat aag bujhane ke liye hain
ankhon men jo bhar loge to kanton se chubhenge
ye khvab to palkon pe sajane ke liye hain
dekhun tire hathon ko to lagta hai tire haath
mandir men faqat diip jalane ke liye hain
ye ilm ka sauda ye risale ye kitaben
ik shakhs ki yadon ko bhulane ke liye hain

aahat si koi aae to lagta hai ki tum ho
saaya koi lahrae to lagta hai ki tum ho
jab shakh koi haath lagate hi chaman men
sharmae lachak jaae to lagta hai ki tum ho
sandal se mahakti hui purkaif hava ka
jhonka koi takrae to lagta hai ki tum ho
odhe hue taron ki chamakti hui chadar
naddi koi bal khaae to lagta hai ki tum ho
jab raat gae koi kiran mere barabar
chupchap si so jaae to lagta hai ki tum ho

bahut dil kar ke honton ki shagufta tazgi di hai
chaman manga tha par us ne bamushkil ik kali di hai
mire khalvatkade ke raat din yunhi nahin sanvre
kisi ne dhuup bakhshi hai kisi ne chandni di hai
nazar ko sabz maidanon ne kya kya vusaten bakhshin
pighalte absharon ne hamen dariyadili di hai
mohabbat narava taqsim ki qaael nahin phir bhi
miri ankhon ko aansu tere honton ko hansi di hai
miri avargi bhi ik karishma hai zamane men
har ik darvesh ne mujh ko duaekhair hi di hai
kahan mumkin tha koi kaam ham jaise divanon se
tumhin ne giit likhvae tumhin ne shairi di hai

ankhen chura ke ham se bahar aae ye nahin
hisse men apne sirf ghubar aae ye nahin
kueghamehayat men sab umr kaat di
thoda sa vaqt vaan bhi guzar aae ye nahin
khud ishq qurbejism bhi hai qurbejan ke saath
ham duur hi se un ko pukar aae ye nahin
ankhon men dil khule hon to mausam ki qaid kya
faslebahar hi men bahar aae ye nahin
ab kya karen ki husn jahan hai aziiz hai
tere siva kisi pe na pyaar aae ye nahin
vaadon ko khunedil se likho tab to baat hai
kaghaz pe qismaton ko sanvar aae ye nahin
kuchh roz aur kal ki muravvat men kaat len
dil ko yaqinevaadaeyar aae ye nahin

aaj muddat men vo yaad aae hain
dar o divar pe kuchh saae hain
abginon se na takra paae
kohsaron se to takrae hain
zindagi tere havadis ham ko
kuchh na kuchh raah pe le aae hain
sangrezon se khazafparon se
kitne hiire kabhi chun laae hain
itne mayus to halat nahin
log kis vaste ghabrae hain
un ki janib na kisi ne dekha
jo hamen dekh ke sharmae hain

chaunk chaunk uthti hai mahlon ki faza raat gae
kaun deta hai ye galiyon men sada raat gae
ye haqaeq ki chatanon se tarashi duniya
odh leti hai tilismon ki rida raat gae
chubh ke rah jaati hai siine men badan ki khushbu
khol deta hai koi bandeqaba raat gae
aao ham jism ki shamon se ujala kar len
chand nikla bhi to niklega zara raat gae
tu na ab aae to kya aaj talak aati hai
sidhiyon se tire qadmon ki sada raat gae

diida o dil men koi husn bikharta hi raha
laakh pardon men chhupa koi sanvarta hi raha
raushni kam na hui vaqt ke tufanon men
dil ke dariya men koi chand utarta hi raha
raste bhar koi aahat thi ki aati hi rahi
koi saaya mire baazu se guzarta hi raha
mit gaya par tiri banhon ne sameta na mujhe
shahr dar shahr main galiyon men bikharta hi raha
lamha lamha rahe ankhon men andhere lekin
koi suraj mire siine men ubharta hi raha

achchha hai un se koi taqaza kiya na jaae
apni nazar men aap ko rusva kiya na jaae
ham hain tira khayal hai tera jamal hai
ik pal bhi apne aap ko tanha kiya na jaae
uthne ko uth to jaaen tiri anjuman se ham
par teri anjuman ko bhi suuna kiya na jaae
un ki ravish juda hai hamari ravish juda
ham se to baat baat pe jhagda kiya na jaae
harchand etibar men dhoke bhi hain magar
ye to nahin kisi pe bharosa kiya na jaae
lahja bana ke baat karen un ke samne
ham se to is tarah ka tamasha kiya na jaae
inaam ho khitab ho vaise mile kahan
jab tak sifarishon ko ikattha kiya na jaae
is vaqt ham se puchh na gham rozgar ke
ham se har ek ghunt ko kadva kiya na jaae

dil ko har lamha bachate rahe jazbat se ham
itne majbur rahe hain kabhi halat se ham
nashshaemai se kahin pyaas bujhi hai dil ki
tishnagi aur badha laae kharajat se ham
aaj to mil ke bhi jaise na mile hon tujh se
chaunk uthte the kabhi teri mulaqat se ham
ishq men aaj bhi hai nimnigahi ka chalan
pyaar karte hain usi husnerivayat se ham
markazedidaekhubanejahan hain bhi to kya
ek nisbat bhi to rakhte hain tiri zaat se ham

ai dardeishq tujh se mukarne laga huun main
mujh ko sambhal had se guzarne laga huun main
pahle haqiqaton hi se matlab tha aur ab
ek aadh baat farz bhi karne laga huun main
har aan tutte ye aqidon ke silsile
lagta hai jaise aaj bikharne laga huun main
ai chashmeyar mera sudharna muhal tha
tera kamal hai ki sudharne laga huun main
ye mehromah arzosama mujh men kho gae
ik kaenat ban ke ubharne laga huun main
itnon ka pyaar mujh se sambhala na jaega
logo tumhare pyaar se darne laga huun main
dilli kahan gaiin tire kuchon ki raunaqen
galiyon se sar jhuka ke guzarne laga huun main

ham ne kaati hain tiri yaad men raten aksar
dil se guzri hain sitaron ki baraten aksar
aur to kaun hai jo mujh ko tasalli deta
haath rakh deti hain dil par tiri baten aksar
husn shaistaetahzibealam hai shayad
ghamzada lagti hain kyuun chandni raten aksar
haal kahna hai kisi se to mukhatab hai koi
kitni dilchasp hua karti hain baten aksar
ishq rahzan na sahi ishq ke hathon phir bhi
ham ne lutti hui dekhi hain baraten aksar
ham se ik baar bhi jiita hai na jitega koi
vo to ham jaan ke kha lete hain maten aksar
un se puchho kabhi chehre bhi padhe hain tum ne
jo kitabon ki kiya karte hain baten aksar
ham ne un tundhavaon men jalae hain charagh
jin havaon ne ulat di hain bisaten aksar

ham se bhaga na karo duur ghazalon ki tarah
ham ne chaha hai tumhen chahne valon ki tarah
khudbakhud niind si ankhon men ghuli jaati hai
mahki mahki hai shabegham tire balon ki tarah
tere bin raat ke hathon pe ye taron ke ayagh
khubsurat hain magar zahr ke pyalon ki tarah
aur kya is se ziyada koi narmi bartun
dil ke zakhmon ko chhua hai tire galon ki tarah
gungunate hue aur aa kabhi un sinon men
teri khatir jo mahakte hain shivalon ki tarah
teri zulfen tiri ankhen tire abru tire lab
ab bhi mashhur hain duniya men misalon ki tarah
ham se mayus na ho ai shabedauran ki abhi
dil men kuchh dard chamakte hain ujalon ki tarah
mujh se nazren to milao ki hazaron chehre
meri ankhon men sulagte hain savalon ki tarah
aur to mujh ko mila kya miri mehnat ka sila
chand sikke hain mire haath men chhalon ki tarah
justuju ne kisi manzil pe thaharne na diya
ham bhatakte rahe avara khayalon ki tarah
zindagi jis ko tira pyaar mila vo jaane
ham to nakam rahe chahne valon ki tarah

har ek ruuh men ik gham chhupa lage hai mujhe
ye zindagi to koi baddua lage hai mujhe
pasandekhatireahlevafa hai muddat se
ye dil ka daagh jo khud bhi bhala lage hai mujhe
jo ansuon men kabhi raat bhiig jaati hai
bahut qarib vo avazepa lage hai mujhe
main so bhi jaun to kya meri band ankhon men
tamam raat koi jhankta lage hai mujhe
main jab bhi us ke khayalon men kho sa jaata huun
vo khud bhi baat kare to bura lage hai mujhe
main sochta tha ki lautunga ajnabi ki tarah
ye mera gaanv to pahchanta lage hai mujhe
na jaane vaqt ki raftar kya dikhati hai
kabhi kabhi to bada khauf sa lage hai mujhe
bikhar gaya hai kuchh is tarah aadmi ka vajud
har ek fard koi saneha lage hai mujhe
ab ek aadh qadam ka hisab kya rakhiye
abhi talak to vahi fasla lage hai mujhe
hikayateghamedil kuchh kashish to rakhti hai
zamana ghaur se sunta hua lage hai mujhe

har ek shakhs pareshanodarbadar sa lage
ye shahr mujh ko to yaaro koi bhanvar sa lage
ab us ke tarzetajahul ko kya kahe koi
vo bekhabar to nahin phir bhi bekhabar sa lage
har ek gham ko khushi ki tarah baratna hai
ye daur vo hai ki jiina bhi ik hunar sa lage
nashatesohbaterindan bahut ghanimat hai
ki lamha lamha purashobopurkhatar sa lage
kise khabar hai ki duniya ka hashr kya hoga
kabhi kabhi to mujhe aadmi se dar sa lage
vo tund vaqt ki rau hai ki paanv tik na saken
har aadmi koi ukhda hua shajar sa lage
jahanenau ke mukammal singar ki khatir
sadi sadi ka zamana bhi mukhtasar sa lage

hausla kho na diya teri nahin se ham ne
kitni shiknon ko chuna teri jabin se ham ne
vo bhi kya din the ki divana bane phirte the
sun liya tha tire baare men kahin se ham ne
jis jagah pahlepahal naam tira aata hai
dastan apni sunai hai vahin se ham ne
yuun to ehsan hasinon ke uthae hain bahut
pyaar lekin jo kiya hai to tumhin se ham ne
kuchh samajh kar hi khuda tujh ko kaha hai varna
kaun si baat kahi itne yaqin se ham ne

jab lagen zakhm to qatil ko dua di jaae
hai yahi rasm to ye rasm utha di jaae
dil ka vo haal hua hai ghamedauran ke tale
jaise ik laash chatanon men daba di jaae
inhin gulrang darichon se sahar jhankegi
kyuun na khilte hue zakhmon ko dua di jaae
kam nahin nashshe men jaade ki gulabi raten
aur agar teri javani bhi mila di jaae
ham se puchho ki ghazal kya hai ghazal ka fan kya
chand lafzon men koi aag chhupa di jaae

jism ki har baat hai avargi ye mat kaho
ham bhi kar sakte hain aisi shaeri ye mat kaho
us nazar ki us badan ki gungunahat to suno
ek si hoti hai har ik ragni ye mat kaho
ham se divanon ke bin duniya sanvarti kis tarah
aql ke aage hai kya divangi ye mat kaho
kat saki hain aaj tak sone ki zanjiren kahan
ham bhi ab azad hain yaaro abhi ye mat kaho
paanv itne tez hain uthte nazar aate nahin
aaj thak kar rah gaya hai aadmi ye mat kaho
jitne vaade kal the utne aaj bhi maujud hain
un ke vaadon men hui hai kuchh kami ye mat kaho
dil men apne dard ki chhitki hui hai chandni
har taraf phaili hui hai tirgi ye mat kaho

khudbakhud mai hai ki shishe men bhari aave hai
kis bala ki tumhen jadunazari aave hai
dil men dar aave hai har subh koi yaad aise
juun dabepanv nasimesahari aave hai
aur bhi zakhm hue jaate hain gahre dil ke
ham to samjhe the tumhen charagari aave hai
ek qatra bhi lahu jab na rahe siine men
tab kahin ishq men kuchh bejigari aave hai
chakedamanogireban ke bhi adab hain kuchh
har divane ko kahan jamadari aave hai
shajareishq to mange hai lahu ke aansu
tab kahin ja ke koi shakh hari aave hai
tu kabhi raag kabhi rang kabhi khushbu hai
kaisi kaisi na tujhe ishvagari aave hai
apapne ko bhulana koi asan nahin
badi mushkil se miyan bekhabari aave hai
ai mire shahrenigaran tira kya haal hua
chappe chappe pe mire aankh bhari aave hai
sahibo husn ki pahchan koi khel nahin
dil lahu ho to kahin didavari aave hai

laakh avara sahi shahron ke futpathon pe ham
laash ye kis ki liye phirte hain in hathon pe ham
ab unhin baton ko sunte hain to aati hai hansi
betarah iman le aae the jin baton pe ham
koi bhi mausam ho dil ki aag kam hoti nahin
muft ka ilzam rakh dete barsaton pe ham
zulf se chhanti hui us ke badan ki tabishen
hans diya karte the aksar chandni raton pe ham
ab unhen pahchante bhi sharm aati hai hamen
fakhr karte the kabhi jin ki mulaqaton pe ham

log kahte hain ki tu ab bhi khafa hai mujh se
teri ankhon ne to kuchh aur kaha hai mujh se
haae us vaqt ko kosun ki dua duun yaaro
jis ne har dard mira chhin liya hai mujh se
dil ka ye haal ki dhadke hi chala jaata hai
aisa lagta hai koi jurm hua hai mujh se
kho gaya aaj kahan rizq ka dene vaala
koi roti jo khada maang raha hai mujh se
ab mire qatl ki tadbir to karni hogi
kaun sa raaz hai tera jo chhupa hai mujh se

maana ki rang rang tira pairahan bhi hai
par is men kuchh karishmaeaksebadan bhi hai
aqlemaash o hikmateduniya ke bavajud
ham ko aziiz ishq ka divanapan bhi hai
mutrib bhi tu nadim bhi tu saqiya bhi tu
tu janeanjuman hi nahin anjuman bhi hai
baazu chhua jo tu ne to us din khula ye raaz
tu sirf rangobu hi nahin hai badan bhi hai
ye daur kis tarah se katega pahad sa
yaaro batao ham men koi kohkan bhi hai

maikashi ab miri aadat ke siva kuchh bhi nahin
ye bhi ik talkh haqiqat ke siva kuchh bhi nahin
fitnaeaql ke juuya miri duniya se guzar
meri duniya men mohabbat ke siva kuchh bhi nahin
dil men vo shorishejazbat kahan tere baghair
ek khamosh qayamat ke siva kuchh bhi nahin
mujh ko khud apni javani ki qasam hai ki ye ishq
ik javani ki shararat ke siva kuchh bhi nahin

maujegul maujesaba maujesahar lagti hai
sar se pa tak vo saman hai ki nazar lagti hai
ham ne har gaam pe sajdon ke jalae hain charagh
ab hamen teri gali rahguzar lagti hai
lamhe lamhe men basi hai tiri yadon ki mahak
aaj ki raat to khushbu ka safar lagti hai
jal gaya apna nasheman to koi baat nahin
dekhna ye hai ki ab aag kidhar lagti hai
saari duniya men gharibon ka lahu bahta hai
har zamin mujh ko mire khuun se tar lagti hai
koi asuda nahin ahlesiyasat ke siva
ye sadi dushmanearbabehunar lagti hai
vaqia shahr men kal to koi aisa na hua
ye to akhbar ke daftar ki khabar lagti hai
lucknow kya tiri galiyon ka muqaddar tha yahi
har gali aaj tiri khakbasar lagti hai

muddat hui us janehaya ne ham se ye iqrar kiya
jitne bhi badnam hue ham utna us ne pyaar kiya
pahle bhi khushchashmon men ham chaukanna se rahte the
teri soi ankhon ne to aur hamen hoshiyar kiya
jaate jaate koi ham se achchhe rahna kah to gaya
puchhe lekin puchhne vaale kis ne ye bimar kiya
qatra qatra sirf hua hai ishq men apne dil ka lahu
shakl dikhai tab us ne jab ankhon ko khunbar kiya
ham par kitni baar pade ye daure bhi tanhai ke
jo bhi ham se milne aaya milne se inkar kiya
ishq men kya nuqsan nafa hai ham ko kya samjhate ho
ham ne saari umr hi yaaro dil ka karobar kiya
mahfil par jab niind si chhai sab ke sab khamosh hue
ham ne tab kuchh sher sunaya logon ko bedar kiya
ab tum socho ab tum jaano jo chaho ab rang bharo
ham ne to ik naqsha khincha ik khaka tayyar kiya
desh se jab pardesh sidhare ham par ye bhi vaqt pada
nazmen chhodi ghazlen chhodi giton ka bevpar kiya

mujhe maalum hai main saari duniya ki amanat huun
magar vo lamha jab main sirf apna ho sa jaata huun
main tum se duur rahta huun to mere saath rahti ho
tumhare paas aata huun to tanha ho sa jaata huun
main chahe sach hi bolun har tarah se apne baare men
magar tum muskurati ho to jhuta ho sa jaata huun
tire gulrang honton se dahakti zindagi pi kar
main pyasa aur pyasa aur pyasa ho sa jaata huun
tujhe banhon men bhar lene ki khvahish yuun ubharti hai
ki main apni nazar men aap rusva ho sa jaata huun

ranjogham mange hai andohobala mange hai
dil vo mujrim hai ki khud apni saza mange hai
chup hai har zakhmegulu chup hai shahidon ka lahu
dasteqatil hai jo mehnat ka sila mange hai
tu bhi ik daulatenayab hai par kya kahiye
zindagi aur bhi kuchh tere siva mange hai
khoi khoi ye nigahen ye khamida palken
haath uthae koi jis tarah dua mange hai
raas ab aaegi ashkon ki na aahon ki faza
aaj ka pyaar nai abohava mange hai
bansuri ka koi naghma na sahi chikh sahi
har sukuteshabegham koi sada mange hai
laakh munkir sahi par zauqeparastish mera
aaj bhi koi sanam koi khuda mange hai
saans vaise hi zamane ki ruki jaati hai
vo badan aur bhi kuchh tang qaba mange hai
dil har ik haal se begana hua jaata hai
ab tavajjoh na taghaful na ada mange hai

sau chand bhi chamkenge to kya baat banegi
tum aae to is raat ki auqat banegi
un se yahi kah aaen ki ab ham na milenge
akhir koi taqribemulaqat banegi
ai navakegham dil men hai ik buund lahu ki
kuchh aur to kya ham se mudarat banegi
ye ham se na hoga ki kisi ek ko chahen
ai ishq hamari na tire saat banegi
ye kya hai ki badhte chalo badhte chalo aage
jab baith ke sochenge to kuchh baat banegi

subh ke dard ko raton ki jalan ko bhulen
kis ke ghar jaaen ki is vaadashikan ko bhulen
aaj tak chot dabae nahin dabti dil ki
kis tarah us sanamesangbadan ko bhulen
ab siva is ke mudavaeghamedil kya hai
itni pi jaaen ki har ranjomehan ko bhulen
aur tahzibeghameishq nibha den kuchh din
akhiri vaqt men kya apne chalan ko bhulen

tamam umr azabon ka silsila to raha
ye kam nahin hamen jiine ka hausla to raha
guzar hi aae kisi tarah tere divane
qadam qadam pe koi sakht marhala to raha
chalo na ishq hi jiita na aql haar saki
tamam vaqt maze ka muqabla to raha
main teri zaat men gum ho saka na tu mujh men
bahut qarib the ham phir bhi fasla to raha
ye aur baat ki har chhed laubali thi
tiri nazar ka dilon se moamla to raha

tuluesubh hai nazren utha ke dekh zara
shikastezulmateshab muskura ke dekh zara
ghamebahar o ghameyar hi nahin sab kuchh
ghamejahan se bhi dil ko laga ke dekh zara
bahar kaun si saughat le ke aai hai
hamare zakhmetamanna tu aa ke dekh zara
har ek samt se ik aftab ubhrega
charaghedairoharam to bujha ke dekh zara
vajudeishq ki tarikh ka pata to chale
varaq ulat ke tu arz o sama ke dekh zara
mile to tu hi mile aur kuchh qubul nahin
jahan men hausle ahlevafa ke dekh zara
tiri nazar se hai rishta mire gireban ka
kidhar hai meri taraf muskura ke dekh zara

tumhare jashn ko jashnefarozan ham nahin kahte
lahu ki garm bundon ko charaghan ham nahin kahte
agar had se guzar jaae dava to ban nahin jaata
kisi bhi dard ko duniya ka darman ham nahin kahte
nazar ki intiha koi na dil ki intiha koi
kisi bhi husn ko husnefaravan ham nahin kahte
kisi ashiq ke shane par bikhar jaae to kya kahna
magar is zulf ko zulfepareshan ham nahin kahte
na buegul mahakti hai na shakhegul lachakti hai
abhi apne gulistan ko gulistan ham nahin kahte
baharon se junun ko har tarah nisbat sahi lekin
shaguftegul ko ashiq ka gareban ham nahin kahte
hazaron saal biite hain hazaron saal bitenge
badal jaegi kal taqdireinsan ham nahin kahte

tum pe kya biit gai kuchh to batao yaaro
main koi ghair nahin huun ki chhupao yaaro
in andheron se nikalne ki koi raah karo
khunedil se koi mishal hi jalao yaaro
ek bhi khvab na ho jin men vo ankhen kya hain
ik na ik khvab to ankhon men basao yaaro
bojh duniya ka uthaunga akela kab tak
ho sake tum se to kuchh haath batao yaaro
zindagi yuun to na banhon men chali aaegi
ghamedauran ke zara naaz uthao yaaro
umrbhar qatl hua huun main tumhari khatir
akhiri vaqt to suuli na chadhao yaaro
aur kuchh der tumhen dekh ke ji luun thahro
meri balin se abhi uth ke na jaao yaaro

tu is qadar mujhe apne qarib lagta hai
tujhe alag se jo sochun ajiib lagta hai
jise na husn se matlab na ishq se sarokar
vo shakhs mujh ko bahut badnasib lagta hai
hududezat se bahar nikal ke dekh zara
na koi ghair na koi raqib lagta hai
ye dosti ye marasim ye chahaten ye khulus
kabhi kabhi mujhe sab kuchh ajiib lagta hai
ufuq pe duur chamakta hua koi taara
mujhe charaghedayarehabib lagta hai

ufuq agarche pighalta dikhai padta hai
mujhe to duur savera dikhai padta hai
hamare shahr men bechehra log baste hain
kabhi kabhi koi chehra dikhai padta hai
chalo ki apni mohabbat sabhi ko baant aaen
har ek pyaar ka bhuka dikhai padta hai
jo apni zaat se ik anjuman kaha jaae
vo shakhs tak mujhe tanha dikhai padta hai
na koi khvab na koi khalish na koi khumar
ye aadmi to adhura dikhai padta hai
lachak rahi hain shuaon ki sidhiyan paiham
falak se koi utarta dikhai padta hai
chamakti ret pe ye ghusleaftab tira
badan tamam sunahra dikhai padta hai

vo ham se aaj bhi damankashan chale hai miyan
kisi pe zor hamara kahan chale hai miyan
jahan bhi thak ke koi karvan thaharta hai
vahin se ek naya karvan chale hai miyan
jo ek samt guman hai to ek samt yaqin
ye zindagi to yunhi darmiyan chale hai miyan
badalte rahte hain bas naam aur to kya hai
hazaron saal se ik dastan chale hai miyan
har ik qadam hai nai azmaishon ka hujum
tamam umr koi imtihan chale hai miyan
vahin pe ghumte rahna to koi baat nahin
zamin chale hai to aage kahan chale hai miyan
vo ek lamhaehairat ki lafz saath na den
nahin chale hai na aise men haan chale hai miyan

vo log hi har daur men mahbub rahe hain
jo ishq men talib nahin matlub rahe hain
tufan ki avaz to aati nahin lekin
lagta hai safine se kahin duub rahe hain
un ko na pukaro ghamedauran ke laqab se
jo dard kisi naam se mansub rahe hain
ham bhi tiri surat ke parastar hain lekin
kuchh aur bhi chehre hamen marghub rahe hain
alfaz men izharemohabbat ke tariqe
khud ishq ki nazron men bhi mayub rahe hain
is ahdebasirat men bhi naqqad hamare
har ek bade naam se marub rahe hain
itna bhi na ghabrao nai tarzeada se
har daur men badle hue uslub rahe hain

zamin hogi kisi qatil ka daman ham na kahte the
akarat jaega khuneshahidan ham na kahte the
ilajechakepairahan hua to is tarah hoga
siya jaega kanton se gareban ham na kahte the
tarane kuchh diye lafzon men khud ko qaid kar lenge
ajab andaz se phailega zindan ham na kahte the
koi itna na hoga laash bhi le ja ke dafna de
inhin sadkon pe mar jaega insan ham na kahte the
nazar lipti hai sholon men lahu tapta hai ankhon men
utha hi chahta hai koi tufan ham na kahte the
chhalakte jaam men bhigi hui ankhen utar aaiin
sataegi kisi din yadeyaran ham na kahte the
nai tahzib kaise lucknow ko raas aaegi
ujad jaega ye shahreghazalan ham na kahte the

zara si baat pe har rasm tod aaya tha
diletabah ne bhi kya mizaj paaya tha
guzar gaya hai koi lamhaesharar ki tarah
abhi to main use pahchan bhi na paaya tha
muaaf kar na saki meri zindagi mujh ko
vo ek lamha ki main tujh se tang aaya tha
shagufta phuul simat kar kali bane jaise
kuchh is kamal se tu ne badan churaya tha
pata nahin ki mire baad un pe kya guzri
main chand khvab zamane men chhod aaya tha

zindagi tujh ko bhulaya hai bahut din ham ne
vaqt khvabon men ganvaya hai bahut din ham ne
ab ye neki bhi hamen jurm nazar aati hai
sab ke aibon ko chhupaya hai bahut din ham ne
tum bhi is dil ko dukha lo to koi baat nahin
apna dil aap dukhaya hai bahut din ham ne
muddaton tarketamanna pe lahu roya hai
ishq ka qarz chukaya hai bahut din ham ne
kya pata ho bhi sake is ki talafi ki nahin
shaeri tujh ko ganvaya hai bahut din ham ne

zindagi ye to nahin tujh ko sanvara hi na ho
kuchh na kuchh ham ne tira qarz utara hi na ho
dil ko chhu jaati hai yuun raat ki avaz kabhi
chaunk uthta huun kahin tu ne pukara hi na ho
kabhi palkon pe chamakti hai jo ashkon ki lakir
sochta huun tire anchal ka kinara hi na ho
zindagi ek khalish de ke na rah ja mujh ko
dard vo de jo kisi tarah gavara hi na ho
sharm aati hai ki us shahr men ham hain ki jahan
na mile bhiik to lakhon ka guzara hi na ho

zulfen siina naaf kamar
ek nadi men kitne bhanvar
sadiyon sadiyon mera safar
manzil manzil rahguzar
kitna mushkil kitna kathin
jiine se jiine ka hunar
gaanv men aa kar shahr base
gaanv bichare jaaen kidhar
phunkne vaale socha bhi
phailegi ye aag kidhar
laakh tarah se naam tira
baitha likkhun kaghaz par
chhote chhote zehn ke log
ham se un ki baat na kar
pet pe patthar bandh na le
haath men sajte hain patthar
raat ke pichhe raat chale
khvab hua har khvabesahar
shab bhar to avara phire
laut chalen ab apne ghar

aag hai phaili hui kaali ghataon ki jagah
badduaen hain labon par ab duaon ki jagah
intikhabeahlegulshan par bahut rota hai dil
dekh kar zaghozaghan ko khushnavaon ki jagah

rahzan hote agar un rahnumaon ki jagah
lut gai is daur men ahleqalam ki aabru
bik rahe hain ab sahafi besavaon ki jagah
kuchh to aata ham ko bhi jaan se guzarne ka maza
ghair hote kaash jalib ashnaon ki jagah

bahut raushan hai shamegham hamari
kisi ki yaad hai hamdam hamari
ghalat hai lataalluq hain chaman se
tumhare phuul aur shabnam hamari
ye palkon par nae aansu nahin hain
azal se aankh hai purnam hamari
har ik lab par tabassum dekhne ki
tamanna kab hui hai kam hamari
kahi hai ham ne khud se bhi bahut kam
na puchho dastanegham hamari

ab teri zarurat bhi bahut kam hai miri jaan
ab shauq ka kuchh aur hi aalam hai miri jaan
ab tazkiraekhandaegul baar hai ji par
jaan vaqfeghamegiriyaeshabnam hai miri jaan
rukh par tire bikhri hui ye zulfesiyahtab
tasvirepareshaniealam hai miri jaan
ye kya ki tujhe bhi hai zamane se shikayat
ye kya ki tiri aankh bhi purnam hai miri jaan

mayus na ho aur koi dam hai miri jaan
ye teri tavajjoh ka hai ejaaz ki mujh se
har shakhs tire shahr ka barham hai miri jaan
ai nuzhatemahtab tira gham hai miri ziist
ai nazishekhurshid tira gham hai miri jaan

bate rahoge to apna yunhi bahega lahu
hue na ek to manzil na ban sakega lahu
ho kis ghamand men ai lakht lakht didavaro
tumhen bhi qatilemehnatkashan kahega lahu
isi tarah se agar tum anaparast rahe
khud apna rahnuma aap hi banega lahu
suno tumhare gareban bhi nahin mahfuz
daro tumhara bhi ik din hisab lega lahu
agar na ahd kiya ham ne ek hone ka
ghanim sab ka yunhi bechta rahega lahu
kabhi kabhi mire bachche bhi mujh se puchhte hain
kahan tak aur tu khushk apna hi karega lahu
sada kaha yahi main ne qaribtar hai vo duur
ki jis men koi hamara na pi sakega lahu

afsos tumhen car ke shishe ka hua hai
parva nahin ik maan ka jo dil tuut gaya hai
hota hai asar tum pe kahan nalaegham ka
barham jo hui bazmetarab is ka gila hai
firaun bhi namrud bhi guzre hain jahan men
rahta hai yahan kaun yahan kaun raha hai
tum zulm kahan tak taheaflak karoge
ye baat na bhulo ki hamara bhi khuda hai
azadieinsan ke vahin phuul khilenge
jis ja pe zahir aaj tira khuun gira hai
tachand rahegi ye shabegham ki siyahi
rasta koi suraj ka kahin rok saka hai
tu aaj ka shair hai to kar meri tarah baat
jaise mire honton pe mire dil ki sada hai

apnon ne vo ranj diye hain begane yaad aate hain
dekh ke us basti ki halat virane yaad aate hain
us nagri men qadam qadam pe sar ko jhukana padta hai
us nagri men qadam qadam par butkhane yaad aate hain
ankhen purnam ho jaati hain ghurbat ke sahraon men
jab us rimjhim ki vaadi ke afsane yaad aate hain
aise aise dard mile hain nae dayaron men ham ko
bichhde hue kuchh log purane yarane yaad aate hain
jin ke karan aaj hamare haal pe duniya hasti hai
kitne zalim chehre jaane pahchane yaad aate hain
yuun na luti thi galiyon daulat apne ashkon ki
rote hain to ham ko apne ghamkhane yaad aate hain
koi to parcham le kar nikle apne gareban ka jalib
charon janib sannata hai divane yaad aate hain

bhula bhi de use jo baat ho gai pyare
nae charagh jala raat ho gai pyare
tiri nigahepasheman ko kaise dekhunga
kabhi jo tujh se mulaqat ho gai pyare
na teri yaad na duniya ka gham na apna khayal
ajiib suratehalat ho gai pyare
udaas udaas hain shamen bujhe bujhe saghar
ye kaisi shamekharabat ho gai pyare
vafa ka naam na lega koi zamane men
ham ahledil ko agar maat ho gai pyare
tumhen to naaz bahut doston pe tha jalib
alagthalag se ho kya baat ho gai pyare

baten to kuchh aisi hain ki khud se bhi na ki jaaen
socha hai khamoshi se har ik zahr ko pi jaaen
apna to nahin koi vahan puchhne vaala
us bazm men jaana hai jinhen ab to vahi jaaen
ab tujh se hamen koi taalluq nahin rakhna
achchha ho ki dil se tiri yaden bhi chali jaaen
ik umr uthae hain sitam ghair ke ham ne
apnon ki to ik pal bhi jafaen na sahi jaaen
jalib ghamedauran ho ki yaderukhejanan
tanha mujhe rahne den mire dil se sabhi jaaen

aur sab bhuul gae harfesadaqat likhna

dil ki baat labon par la kar ab tak ham dukh sahte hain
