jis insan ne apna hi jalva na dekha
bahut shor sunte the is anjuman ka
yahan aa ke jo kuchh suna tha na dekha
safai hai baghemohabbat men aisi
ki badesaba ne bhi tinka na dekha
use dekh kar aur ko phir jo dekhe
koi dekhne vaala aisa na dekha
vo tha jalvaara magar tu ne muusa
na dekha na dekha na dekha na dekha
gaya karvan chhod kar mujh ko tanha
zara mere aane ka rasta na dekha
kahan naqsheavval kahan naqshesani
khuda ki khudai men tujh sa na dekha
tiri yaad hai ya hai tera tasavvur
kabhi dagh ko ham ne tanha na dekha

is ada se vo jafa karte hain
koi jaane ki vafa karte hain
yuun vafa ahdevafa karte hain
aap kya kahte hain kya karte hain
ham ko chhedoge to pachhtaoge
hansne valon se hansa karte hain
namabar tujh ko saliqa hi nahin
kaam baton men bana karte hain
chaliye ashiq ka janaza uttha
aap baithe hue kya karte hain
ye batata nahin koi mujh ko
dil jo aata hai to kya karte hain
husn ka haq nahin rahta baaqi
har ada men vo ada karte hain
tiir akhir badalekafir hai
ham akhir aaj dua karte hain
rote hain ghair ka rona pahron
ye hansi mujh se hansa karte hain
is liye dil ko laga rakkha hai
is men mahbub raha karte hain
tum miloge na vahan bhi ham se
hashr se pahle gila karte hain
jhank kar rauzanedar se mujh ko
kya vo shokhi se haya karte hain
us ne ehsan jata kar ye kaha
aap kis munh se gila karte hain
roz lete hain naya dil dilbar
nahin malum ye kya karte hain
dagh tu dekh to kya hota hai
jabr par sabr kiya karte hain

is nahin ka koi ilaaj nahin
roz kahte hain aap aaj nahin
kal jo tha aaj vo mizaj nahin
is talavvun ka kuchh ilaaj nahin
aaina dekhte hi itrae
phir ye kya hai agar mizaj nahin
le ke dil rakh lo kaam aaega
go abhi tum ko ehtiyaj nahin
ho saken ham mizajdan kyunkar
ham ko milta tira mizaj nahin
chup lagi lalejanfaza ko tire
is masiha ka kuchh ilaaj nahin
dilebemuddaa khuda ne diya
ab kisi shai ki ehtiyaj nahin
khote damon men ye bhi kya thahra
dirhamedagh ka rivaj nahin
beniyazi ki shaan kahti hai
bandagi ki kuchh ehtiyaj nahin
dillagi kijiye raqibon se
is tarah ka mira mizaj nahin
ishq hai padshahealamgir
garche zahir men takhtotaj nahin
dardefurqat ki go dava hai visal
is ke qabil bhi har mizaj nahin
yaas ne kya bujha diya dil ko
ki tadap kaisi ikhtilaj nahin
ham to siratpasand ashiq hain
khubru kya jo khushmizaj nahin
huur se puchhta huun jannat men
is jagah kya buton ka raaj nahin
sabr bhi dil ko dagh de lenge
abhi kuchh is ki ehtiyaj nahin

jalve miri nigah men kaunomakan ke hain
mujh se kahan chhupenge vo aise kahan ke hain
khulte nahin hain raaz jo sozenihan ke hain
kya phutne ke vaste chhale zaban ke hain
karte hain qatl vo talabemaghfirat ke baad
jo the dua ke haath vahi imtihan ke hain
jis roz kuchh sharik hui meri mushtekhak
us roz se zamin pe sitam asman ke hain
baazu dikhae tum ne laga kar hazar haath
puure pade to vo bhi bahut imtihan ke hain
naseh ke samne kabhi sach bolta nahin
meri zaban men rang tumhari zaban ke hain
kaisa javab hazratedil dekhiye zara
paighambar ke haath men tukde zaban ke hain
kya iztirabeshauq ne mujh ko khajil kiya
vo puchhte hain kahiye irade kahan ke hain
ashiq tire adam ko gae kis qadar tabah
puchha har ek ne ye musafir kahan ke hain
harchand dagh ek hi ayyar hai magar
dushman bhi to chhate hue saare jahan ke hain

jo ho sakta hai us se vo kisi se ho nahin sakta
magar dekho to phir kuchh aadmi se ho nahin sakta
mohabbat men kare kya kuchh kisi se ho nahin sakta
mira marna bhi to meri khushi se ho nahin sakta
alag karna raqibon ka ilahi tujh ko asan hai
mujhe mushkil ki meri bekasi se ho nahin sakta
kiya hai vadaefarda unhon ne dekhiye kya ho
yahan sabr o tahammul aaj hi se ho nahin sakta
ye mushtaqeshahadat kis jagah jaaen kise dhunden
ki tera kaam qatil jab tujhi se ho nahin sakta
laga kar tegh qissa paak kijiye dadkhvahon ka
kisi ka faisla kar munsifi se ho nahin sakta
mira dushman bazahir chaar din ko dost hai tera
kisi ka ho rahe ye har kisi se ho nahin sakta
pursish kahoge kya vahan jab yaan ye surat hai
ada ik harfevada nazuki se ho nahin sakta
na kahiye go ki haledil magar rangashna hain ham
ye zahir aap ki kya khamushi se ho nahin sakta
kiya jo ham ne zalim kya karega ghair munh kya hai
kare to sabr aisa aadmi se ho nahin sakta
chaman men naaz bulbul ne kiya jo apni naale par
chatak kar ghuncha bola kya kisi se ho nahin sakta
nahin gar tujh pe qaabu dil hai par kuchh zor ho apna
karun kya ye bhi to nataqati se ho nahin sakta
na rona hai tariqe ka na hansna hai saliqe ka
pareshani men koi kaam ji se ho nahin sakta
hua huun is qadar mahjub arzemuddaa kar ke
ki ab to uzr bhi sharmindagi se ho nahin sakta
ghazab men jaan hai kya kiije badla ranjefurqat ka
badi se kar nahin sakte khushi se ho nahin sakta
maza jo iztirabeshauq se ashiq ko hai hasil
vo taslim o raza o bandagi se ho nahin sakta
khuda jab dost hai ai dagh kya dushman se andesha
hamara kuchh kisi ki dushmani se ho nahin sakta

kaabe ki hai havas kabhi kuebutan ki hai
mujh ko khabar nahin miri mitti kahan ki hai
sun ke mira fasana unhen lutf aa gaya
sunta huun ab ki roz talab qissakhvan ki hai
paighambar ki baat par aapas men ranj kya
meri zaban ki hai na tumhari zaban ki hai
kuchh tazgi ho lazzateazar ke liye
har dam mujhe talash nae asman ki hai
janbar bhi ho gae hain bahut mujh se nimjan
kya gham hai ai tabib jo puuri vahan ki hai
hasrat baras rahi hai hamare mazar par
kahte hain sab ye qabr kisi naujavan ki hai
vaqtekhiramenaz dikha do juda juda
ye chaal hashr ki ye ravish asman ki hai
fursat kahan ki ham se kisi vaqt tu mile
din ghair ka hai raat tire pasban ki hai
qasid ki guftugu se tasalli ho kis tarah
chhupti nahin vo baat jo teri zaban ki hai
jaureraqib o zulmefalak ka nahin khayal
tashvish ek khatirenamehrban ki hai
sun kar mira fasanaegham us ne ye kaha
ho jaae jhuut sach yahi khubi bayan ki hai
daman sambhal bandh kamar astin chadha
khanjar nikal dil men agar imtihan ki hai
har har nafas men dil se nikalne laga ghubar
kya jaane garderah ye kis karvan ki hai
kyunki na aate khuld se aadam zamin par
mauzun vahin vo khuub hai jo sunte jahan ki hai
taqdir se ye puchh raha huun ki ishq men
tadbir koi bhi sitamenagahan ki hai
urdu hai jis ka naam hamin jante hain dagh
hindostan men dhuum hamari zaban ki hai

kahte hain jis ko huur vo insan tumhin to ho
jaati hai jis pe jaan miri jaan tumhin to ho
matlab ki kah rahe hain vo daana hamin to hain
matlab ki puchhte ho vo nadan tumhin to ho
aata hai badezulm tumhin ko to rahm bhi
apne kiye se dil men pasheman tumhin to ho
pachhtaoge bahut mire dil ko ujaad kar
is ghar men aur kaun hai mehman tumhin to ho
ik roz rang laengi ye mehrbaniyan
ham jante the jaan ke khvahan tumhin to ho
dildar o dilfareb dilazar o dilsitan
lakhon men ham kahenge ki haan haan tumhin to ho
karte ho dagh duur se butkhane ko salam
apni tarah ke ek musalman tumhin to ho

kaun sa tairegumgashta use yaad aaya
dekhta bhalta har shakh ko sayyad aaya
mere qaabu men na pahron dilenashad aaya
vo mira bhulne vaala jo mujhe yaad aaya
koi bhula hua andazesitam yaad aaya
ki tabassum tujhe zalim damebedad aaya
laae hain log janaze ki tarah mahshar men
kis musibat se tira kushtaebedad aaya
jazbevahshat tire qurban tira kya kahna
khinch ke rag rag men mire nashtarefassad aaya
us ke jalve ko gharaz kaunomakan se kya tha
daad lene ke liye husnekhudadad aaya
bastiyon se yahi avaz chali aati hai
jo kiya tu ne vo aage tire farhad aaya
dileviran se raqibon ne muraden pain
kaam kis kis ke mira khirmanebarbad aaya
ishq ke aate hi munh par mire phuli hai basant
ho gaya zard ye shagird jab ustad aaya
ho gaya farz mujhe shauq ka daftar likhna
jab mire haath koi khamaefaulad aaya
iid hai qatl mira ahletamasha ke liye
sab gale milne lage jab ki vo jallad aaya
chain karte hain vahan ranj uthane vaale
kaam uqba men hamara dilenashad aaya
di shabevasl moazzin ne azaan pichhli raat
haae kambakht ko kis vaqt khuda yaad aaya
mere naale ne sunai hai khari kis kis ko
munh farishton pe ye gustakh ye azad aaya
ghamejaved ne di mujh ko mubarakbadi
jab suna ye ki unhen shevaebedad aaya
main tamannaeshahadat ka maza bhuul gaya
aaj is shauq se arman se jallad aaya
shadiyana jo diya naala o shevan ne diya
jab mulaqat ko nashad ki nashad aaya
lijiye suniye ab afsanaefurqat mujh se
aap ne yaad dilaya to mujhe yaad aaya
aap ki bazm men sab kuchh hai magar dagh nahin
ham ko vo khanakharab aaj bahut yaad aaya

khatir se ya lihaz se main maan to gaya
jhuti qasam se aap ka iman to gaya
dil le ke muft kahte hain kuchh kaam ka nahin
ulti shikayaten huiin ehsan to gaya
darta huun dekh kar dilebearzu ko main
sunsan ghar ye kyuun na ho mehman to gaya
kya aae rahat aai jo kunjemazar men
vo valvala vo shauq vo arman to gaya
dekha hai butkade men jo ai shaikh kuchh na puchh
iman ki to ye hai ki iman to gaya
ifshaerazeishq men go zillaten huiin
lekin use jata to diya jaan to gaya
go namabar se khush na hua par hazar shukr
mujh ko vo mere naam se pahchan to gaya
bazmeadu men surateparvana dil mira
go rashk se jala tire qurban to gaya
hosh o havas o taab o tavan dagh ja chuke
ab ham bhi jaane vaale hain saman to gaya

le chala jaan miri ruuth ke jaana tera
aise aane se to behtar tha na aana tera
apne dil ko bhi bataun na thikana tera
sab ne jaana jo pata ek ne jaana tera
tu jo ai zulf pareshan raha karti hai
kis ke ujde hue dil men hai thikana tera
aarzu hi na rahi subhevatan ki mujh ko
shameghurbat hai ajab vaqt suhana tera
ye samajh kar tujhe ai maut laga rakkha hai
kaam aata hai bure vaqt men aana tera
ai dileshefta men aag lagane vaale
rang laaya hai ye lakhe ka jamana tera
tu khuda to nahin ai nasehenadan mera
kya khata ki jo kaha main ne na maana tera
ranj kya vasleadu ka jo taalluq hi nahin
mujh ko vallah hansata hai rulana tera
kaaba o dair men ya chashmodileashiq men
inhin dochar gharon men hai thikana tera
tarkeadat se mujhe niind nahin aane ki
kahin nicha na ho ai gor sirhana tera
main jo kahta huun uthae hain bahut ranjefiraq
vo ye kahte hain bada dil hai tavana tera
bazmedushman se tujhe kaun utha sakta hai
ik qayamat ka uthana hai uthana tera
apni ankhon men abhi kaund gai bijli si
ham na samjhe ki ye aana hai ki jaana tera
yuun to kya aaega tu fartenazakat se yahan
sakht dushvar hai dhoke men bhi aana tera
dagh ko yuun vo mitate hain ye farmate hain
tu badal daal hua naam purana tera

lutf vo ishq men paae hain ki ji janta hai
ranj bhi aise uthae hain ki ji janta hai
jo zamane ke sitam hain vo zamana jaane
tu ne dil itne satae hain ki ji janta hai
tum nahin jante ab tak ye tumhare andaz
vo mire dil men samae hain ki ji janta hai
inhin qadmon ne tumhare inhin qadmon ki qasam
khaak men itne milae hain ki ji janta hai
dosti men tiri darparda hamare dushman
is qadar apne parae hain ki ji janta hai

maze ishq ke kuchh vahi jante hain
ki jo maut ko zindagi jante hain
shabevasl liin un ki itni balaen
ki hamdam mire haath hi jante hain
na ho dil to kya lutfeazarorahat
barabar khushi nakhushi jante hain
jo hai mere dil men unhin ko khabar hai
jo main janta huun vahi jante hain
pada huun sarebazm main dam churae
magar vo ise bekhudi jante hain
kahan qadrehamjins hamjins ko hai
farishton ko bhi aadmi jante hain
kahun haledil to kahen us se hasil

vo nadan anjan bhole hain aise
ki sab shevaedushmani jante hain
nahin jante is ka anjam kya hai
vo marna mera dillagi jante hain
samajhta hai tu dagh ko rind zahid
magar rind us ko vali jante hain

milate ho usi ko khaak men jo dil se milta hai
miri jaan chahne vaala badi mushkil se milta hai
kahin hai iid ki shadi kahin matam hai maqtal men
koi qatil se milta hai koi bismil se milta hai
paseparda bhi laila haath rakh leti hai ankhon par
ghubarenatavaneqais jab mahmil se milta hai
bhare hain tujh men vo lakhon hunar ai majmaekhubi

mujhe aata hai kya kya rashk vaqtezabh us se bhi
gala jis dam lipat kar khanjareqatil se milta hai
bazahir baadab yuun hazratenaseh se milta huun
muridekhas jaise murshidekamil se milta hai
misaleganjeqarun ahlehajat se nahin chhupta
jo hota hai sakhi khud dhund kar saail se milta hai
javab is baat ka us shokh ko kya de sake koi
jo dil le kar kahe kambakht tu kis dil se milta hai
chhupae se koi chhupti hai apne dil ki betabi
ki har tarenafas apna ragebismil se milta hai
adam ki jo haqiqat hai vo puchho ahlehasti se
musafir ko to manzil ka pata manzil se milta hai
ghazab hai dagh ke dil se tumhara dil nahin milta
tumhara chand sa chehra mahekamil se milta hai

narava kahiye nasaza kahiye
kahiye kahiye mujhe bura kahiye
tujh ko badahd o bevafa kahiye
aise jhute ko aur kya kahiye
dard dil ka na kahiye ya kahiye
jab vo puchhe mizaj kya kahiye
phir na rukiye jo muddaa kahiye
ek ke baad dusra kahiye
aap ab mera munh na khulvaen
ye na kahiye ki muddaa kahiye
vo mujhe qatl kar ke kahte hain
manta hi na tha ye kya kahiye
dil men rakhne ki baat hai ghameishq
is ko hargiz na barmala kahiye
tujh ko achchha kaha hai kis kis ne
kahne valon ko aur kya kahiye
vo bhi sun lenge ye kabhi na kabhi
haledil sab se jabaja kahiye
mujh ko kahiye bura na ghair ke saath
jo ho kahna juda juda kahiye
intiha ishq ki khuda jaane
dameakhir ko ibtida kahiye
mere matlab se kya gharaz matlab
aap apna to muddaa kahiye
aisi kashti ka dubna achchha
ki jo dushman ko nakhuda kahiye
sabr furqat men aa hi jaata hai
par use derashna kahiye
aa gai aap ko masihai
marne valon ko marhaba kahiye
aap ka khairkhvah mere siva
hai koi aur dusra kahiye
haath rakh kar vo apne kanon par
mujh se kahte hain majra kahiye
hosh jaate rahe raqibon ke
dagh ko aur bavafa kahiye

phire raah se vo yahan aate aate
ajal mar rahi tu kahan aate aate
na jaana ki duniya se jaata hai koi
bahut der ki mehrban aate aate
suna hai ki aata hai sar namabar ka
kahan rah gaya armughan aate aate
yaqin hai ki ho jaae akhir ko sachchi
mire munh men teri zaban aate aate
sunane ke qabil jo thi baat un ko
vahi rah gai darmiyan aate aate
mujhe yaad karne se ye muddaa tha
nikal jaae dam hichkiyan aate aate
abhi sin hi kya hai jo bebakiyan hon
unhen aengi shokhiyan aate aate
kaleja mire munh ko aaega ik din
yunhi lab par ahofughan aate aate
chale aate hain dil men arman lakhon
makan bhar gaya mehman aate aate
natija na nikla thake sab payami
vahan jaate jaate yahan aate aate
tumhara hi mushtaqedidar hoga
gaya jaan se ik javan aate aate
tiri aankh phirte hi kaisa phira hai
miri raah par asman aate aate
pada hai bada pech phir dillagi men
tabiat ruki hai jahan aate aate

bahar aate aate khizan aate aate
nahin khel ai dagh yaron se kah do
ki aati hai urdu zaban aate aate

ranj ki jab guftugu hone lagi
aap se tum tum se tu hone lagi
chahiye paighambar donon taraf
lutf kya jab dubadu hone lagi
meri rusvai ki naubat aa gai
un ki shohrat kubaku hone lagi
hai tiri tasvir kitni behijab
har kisi ke rubaru hone lagi
ghair ke hote bhala ai shamevasl
kyuun hamare rubaru hone lagi
naummidi badh gai hai is qadar
aarzu ki aarzu hone lagi
ab ke mil kar dekhiye kya rang ho
phir hamari justuju hone lagi
dagh itrae hue phirte hain aaj
shayad un ki aabru hone lagi

saaf kab imtihan lete hain
vo to dam de ke jaan lete hain
yuun hai manzur khanavirani
mol mera makan lete hain
tum taghaful karo raqibon se
janne vaale jaan lete hain
phir na aana agar koi bheje
namabar se zaban lete hain
ab bhi gir pad ke zof se naale
satvan asman lete hain
tere khanjar se bhi to ai qatil
nok ki naujavan lete hain
apne bismil ka sar hai zaanu par
kis mohabbat se jaan lete hain
ye suna hai mire liye talvar
ik mire mehrban lete hain
ye na kah ham se tere munh men khaak
is men teri zaban lete hain
kaun jaata hai us gali men jise
duur se pasban lete hain
manzileshauq tai nahin hoti
thekiyan natavan lete hain
kar guzarte hain ho buri ki bhali
dil men jo kuchh vo thaan lete hain
vo jhagadte hain jab raqibon se
biich men mujh ko saan lete hain
zid har ik baat par nahin achchhi
dost ki dost maan lete hain
mustaid ho ke ye kaho to sahi
aaiye imtihan lete hain
dagh bhi hai ajiib sehrbayan
baat jis ki vo maan lete hain

saaz ye kinasaz kya janen
naaz vaale niyaz kya janen
shamaru aap go hue lekin
lutfesozogudaz kya janen
kab kisi dar ki jabhasai ki

jin ko apni khabar nahin ab tak
vo mire dil ka raaz kya janen
hazratekhizr jab shahid na hon
lutfeumredaraz kya janen
jo guzarte hain dagh par sadme
aap bandanavaz kya janen

sabaq aisa padha diya tu ne
dil se sab kuchh bhala diya tu ne
ham nikamme hue zamane ke
kaam aisa sikha diya tu ne
kuchh taalluq raha na duniya se
shaghl aisa bata diya tu ne
kis khushi ki khabar suna ke mujhe
gham ka putla bana diya tu ne
kya bataun ki kya liya main ne
kya kahun main ki kya diya tu ne
betalab jo mila mila mujh ko
begharaz jo diya diya tu ne
umrejaved khizr ko bakhshi
abehaivan pila diya tu ne
narenamrud ko kiya gulzar
dost ko yuun bacha diya tu ne
dastemusa men faiz bakhshish hai
nurolauhoasa diya tu ne
subh mauj nasim gulshan ko
nafasejanfaza diya tu ne
shabetira men shama raushan ko
nuur khurshid ka diya tu ne
naghma bulbul ko rangobu gul ko
dilkashokhushnuma diya tu ne
kahin mushtaq se hijab hua
kahin parda utha diya tu ne
tha mira munh na qabilelabbaik
kaaba mujh ko dikha diya tu ne
jis qadar main ne tujh se khvahish ki
is se mujh ko siva diya tu ne
rahbarekhizrohadieilyas
mujh ko vo rahnuma diya tu ne
mit gae dil se naqshebatil sab
naqsha apna jama diya tu ne
hai yahi raah manzilemaqsud
khuub raste laga diya tu ne
mujh gunahgar ko jo bakhsh diya
to jahannum ko kya diya tu ne
dagh ko kaun dene vaala tha
jo diya ai khuda diya tu ne

sab log jidhar vo hain udhar dekh rahe hain
ham dekhne valon ki nazar dekh rahe hain
tevar tire ai rashkeqamar dekh rahe hain
ham shaam se asaresahar dekh rahe hain
mera dilegumgashta jo dhunda nahin milta
vo apna dahan apni kamar dekh rahe hain
koi to nikal aaega sarbazemohabbat
dil dekh rahe hain vo jigar dekh rahe hain
hai majmaeaghyar ki hangamaemahshar
kya sair mire didaetar dekh rahe hain
ab ai nigaheshauq na rah jaae tamanna
is vaqt udhar se vo idhar dekh rahe hain
harchand ki har roz ki ranjish hai qayamat
ham koi din us ko bhi magar dekh rahe hain
aamad hai kisi ki ki gaya koi idhar se
kyuun sab taraferahguzar dekh rahe hain
takrar tajalli ne tire jalve men kyuun ki
hairatzada sab ahlenazar dekh rahe hain
nairang hai ek ek tira diid ke qabil

tum aina hi na har baar dekhte jaao

tumhare khat men naya ik salam kis ka tha
na tha raqib to akhir vo naam kis ka tha

ye baat baat men kya nazuki nikalti hai
dabi dabi tire lab se hansi nikalti hai
thahar thahar ke jala dil ko ek baar na phunk
ki is men buemohabbat abhi nikalti hai
bajae shikva bhi deta huun main dua us ko
miri zaban se karun kya yahi nikalti hai
khushi men ham ne ye shokhi kabhi nahin dekhi
dameitab jo rangat tiri nikalti hai
hazar baar jo manga karo to kya hasil
dua vahi hai jo dil se kabhi nikalti hai
ada se teri magar khinch rahin hain talvaren
nigah nigah se chhuri par chhuri nikalti hai
muhiteishq men hai kya umiid o biim mujhe
ki duub duub ke kashti miri nikalti hai
jhalak rahi hai sareshakhemizha khuun ki buund
shajar men pahle samar se kali nikalti hai

ye intizar hai kab chandni nikalti hai
samajh to lijiye kahne to dijiye matlab

ye dil ki aag hai ya dil ke nuur ka hai zuhur
nafas nafas men mire raushni nikalti hai
kaha jo main ne ki mar jaunga to kahte hain
hamare zaiche men zindagi nikalti hai
samajhne vaale samajhte hain pech ki taqrir
ki kuchh na kuchh tiri baton men fi nikalti hai
dameakhir tasavvur hai kis parivash ka
ki meri ruuh bhi ban kar pari nikalti hai
sanamkade men bhi hai husn ik khudai ka
ki jo nikalti hai surat pari nikalti hai

jo tum nikalna chaho abhi nikalti hai
ghamefiraq men ho dagh is qadar betab
zara se ranj men jaan aap ki nikalti hai

zahid na kah buri ki ye mastane aadmi hain
tujh ko lipat padenge divane aadmi hain
ghairon ki dosti par kyuun etibar kiije
ye dushmani karenge begane aadmi hain
jo aadmi pe guzri vo ik siva tumhare
kya ji laga ke sunte afsane aadmi hain
kya juraten jo ham ko darban tumhara toke
kah do ki ye to janepahchane aadmi hain
mai buund bhar pila kar kya hans raha hai saaqi
bhar bhar ke piite akhir paimane aadmi hain
tum ne hamare dil men ghar kar liya to kya hai
abad karte akhir virane aadmi hain
naseh se koi kah de kiije kalam aisa
hazrat ko ta ki koi ye jaane aadmi hain
jab davareqayamat puchhega tum pe rakh kar

shabash dagh tujh ko kya tegheishq khaai
ji karte hain vahi jo mardane aadmi hain

ham ne tiri khatir se dilezar bhi chhoda
tu bhi na hua yaar aur ik yaar bhi chhoda
kya hoga rafugar se rafu mera gareban
ai dastejunun tu ne nahin taar bhi chhoda
diin de ke gaya kufr ke bhi kaam se ashiq
tasbih ke saath us ne to zunnar bhi chhoda
goshe men tiri chashmesiyahmast ke dil ne

kya chhoden asiranemohabbat ko vo jis ne
sadqe men na ik murghegiraftar bhi chhoda
pahunchi miri rusvai ki kyunkar khabar us ko
us shokh ne to dekhna akhbar bhi chhoda
karta tha jo yaan aane ka jhuta kabhi iqrar
muddat se zafar us ne vo iqrar bhi chhoda

baat karni mujhe mushkil kabhi aisi to na thi
jaisi ab hai tiri mahfil kabhi aisi to na thi
le gaya chhin ke kaun aaj tira sabr o qarar
beqarari tujhe ai dil kabhi aisi to na thi
us ki ankhon ne khuda jaane kiya kya jaadu
ki tabiat miri maail kabhi aisi to na thi
akserukhsar ne kis ke hai tujhe chamkaya

ab ki jo rahemohabbat men uthai taklif

paekuban koi zindan men naya hai majnun
aati avazesalasil kabhi aisi to na thi
nigaheyar ko ab kyuun hai taghaful ai dil

jaisi ab ho gai qatil kabhi aisi to na thi
kya sabab tu jo bigadta hai zafar se har baar
khu tiri hurshamail kabhi aisi to na thi

bhari hai dil men jo hasrat kahun to kis se kahun
sune hai kaun musibat kahun to kis se kahun
jo tu ho saaf to kuchh main bhi saaf tujh se kahun
tire hai dil men kudurat kahun to kis se kahun
na kohkan hai na majnun ki the mire hamdard
main apna dardemohabbat kahun to kis se kahun
dil us ko aap diya aap hi pasheman huun
ki sach hai apni nadamat kahun to kis se kahun
kahun main jis se use hove sunte hi vahshat
phir apna qissaevahshat kahun to kis se kahun

tujhe to mujh se adavat kahun to kis se kahun
na mujh ko kahne ki taqat kahun to kya ahval
na us ko sunne ki fursat kahun to kis se kahun
kisi ko dekhta itna nahin haqiqat men
zafar main apni haqiqat kahun to kis se kahun

dekh dil ko mire o kafirebepir na tod
ghar hai allah ka ye is ki to taamir na tod
ghul sada vadievahshat men rakhunga barpa
ai junun dekh mire paanv ki zanjir na tod
dekh tuk ghaur se ainaedil ko mere
is men aata hai nazar alametasvir na tod
tajezar ke liye kyuun shama ka sar kaate hai
rishtaeulfateparvana ko gulgir na tod
apne bismil se ye kahta tha damenaza vo shokh
tha jo kuchh ahd so o ashiqedilgir na tod
raqsebismil ka tamasha mujhe dikhla koi dam
dast o pa maar ke dam tu taheshamshir na tod
saham kar ai zafar us shokh kamandar se kah
khinch kar dekh mire siine se tu tiir na tod

ham ye to nahin kahte ki gham kah nahin sakte
par jo sababeghum hai vo ham kah nahin sakte
ham dekhte hain tum men khuda jaane buto kya
is bhed ko allah ki qasam kah nahin sakte
rusvaejahan karta hai ro ro ke hamen tu
ham tujhe kuchh ai didaenam kah nahin sakte
kya puchhta hai ham se tu ai shokh sitamgar
jo tu ne kiye ham pe sitam kah nahin sakte
hai sabr jinhen talkhkalami ko tumhari
sharbat hi batate hain sam kah nahin sakte
jab kahte hain kuchh baat rukavat ki tire ham
ruk jaata hai ye siine men dam kah nahin sakte
allah re tira roab ki ahvaledil apna
de dete hain ham kar ke raqam kah nahin sakte
tubaebahishti hai tumhara qaderaana
ham kyunkar kahen sarveiram kah nahin sakte
jo ham pe shabehijr men us mahelaqa ke
guzre hain zafar ranj o alam kah nahin sakte

dekho insan khaak ka putla bana kya chiiz hai
bolta hai is men kya vo bolta kya chiiz hai
rubaru us zulf ke damebala kya chiiz hai
us nigah ke samne tireqaza kya chiiz hai
yuun to hain saare butan gharatgareimanodin
ek vo kafir sanam namekhuda kya chiiz hai
jis ne dil mera diya damemohabbat men phansa
vo nahin malum muj ko naseha kya chiiz hai
hove ik qatra jo zahrabemohabbat ka nasib
khizr phir to chashmaeabebaqa kya chiiz hai
marg hi sehat hai us ki marg hi us ka ilaaj
ishq ka bimar kya jaane dava kya chiiz hai
dil mira baitha hai le kar phir mujhi se vo nigar
puchhta hai haath men mere bata kya chiiz hai
khaak se paida hue hain dekh rangarang gul
hai to ye nachiz lekin is men kya kya chiiz hai
jis ki tujh ko justuju hai vo tujhi men hai zafar
dhundta phir phir ke to phir jabaja kya chiiz hai

hava men phirte ho kya hirs aur hava ke liye
ghurur chhod do ai ghafilo khuda ke liye
gira diya hai hamen kis ne chaheulfat men
ham aap duube kisi apne ashna ke liye
jahan men chahiye aivan o qasr shahon ko
ye ek gumbadegardun hai bas gada ke liye
vo aina hai ki jis ko hai hajatesimab
ik iztirab hai kaafi dilesafa ke liye
tapish se dil ka ho kya jaane siine men kya haal
jo tere tiir ka rauzan na ho hava ke liye
tabibeishq ki dukkan men dhundte phirte
ye dardmandemohabbat tiri dava ke liye
jo haath aae zafar khakpaefakhruddin
to main rakhun use ankhon ke tutiya ke liye

galiyan tankhvah thahri hai agar bat jaegi
ashiqon ke ghar mithai lab shakar bat jaegi
rubaru gar hoga yusuf aur tu aa jaega
us ki janib se zulekha ki nazar bat jaegi
rahzanon men nazoghamza ki ye jinsedinodil
juun mataeburda akhir hamdigar bat jaegi
hoga kya gar bol utthe ghair baton men miri
phir tabiat meri ai bedad gar bat jaegi
daulateduniya nahin jaane ki hargiz tere saath
baad tere sab yahin ai bekhabar bat jaegi
kar le ai dil jaan ko bhi ranjogham men tu sharik
ye jo mehnat tujh pe hai kuchh kuchh magar bat jaegi
muung chhati pe jo dalte hain kisi ki dekhna
jutiyon men daal un ki ai zafar bat jaegi

gai yakbayak jo hava palat nahin dil ko mere qarar hai
karun us sitam ko main kya bayan mira gham se siina figar hai
ye reayaehind tabah hui kahun kya jo in pe jafa hui
jise dekha hakimevaqt ne kaha ye bhi qabiledar hai
ye kisi ne zulm bhi hai suna ki di phansi logon ko begunah
vahi kalmagoyon ki samt se abhi dil men un ke bukhar hai
na tha shahredehli ye tha chaman kaho kis tarah ka tha yaan aman
jo khitab tha vo mita diya faqat ab to ujda dayar hai
yahi tang haal jo sab ka hai ye karishma qudraterab ka hai
jo bahar thi so khizan hui jo khizan thi ab vo bahar hai
shaboroz phuul men jo tule kaho kharegham ko vo kya sahe
mile tauq qaid men jab unhen kaha gul ke badle ye haar hai
sabhi jaada matamesakht hai kaho kaisi gardishebakht hai
na vo taaj hai na vo takht hai na vo shaah hai na dayar hai
jo suluk karte the aur se vahi ab hain kitne zalil se
vo hain tang charkh ke jaur se raha tan pe un ke na taar hai
na vabal tan pe hai sar mira nahin jaan jaane ka dar zara
kate gham hii nikle jo dam mira mujhe apni zindagi baar hai
kya hai gham zafar tujhe hashr ka jo khuda ne chaha to barmala
hamen hai vasila rasul ka vo hamara hamiekar hai

hai dil ko jo yaad aai falakepir kisi ki
ankhon ke tale phirti hai tasvir kisi ki
girya bhi hai naala bhi hai aur ahofughan bhi
par dil men hui us ke na tasir kisi ki
haath aae hai kya khaak tire khakekafepa
jab tak ki na qismat men ho iksir kisi ki
yaaro vo hai bigda hua baten na banao
kuchh pesh nahin jaane ki taqrir kisi ki
nazan na ho munim ki jahan tera mahal hai
hovegi yahan pahle bhi taamir kisi ki
meri girahedil na khuli hai na khulegi
jab tak na khule zulfegirahgir kisi ki
aata bhi agar hai to vo phir jaae hai ulta
jis vaqt ulat jaae hai taqdir kisi ki
is abru o mizhgan se zafar tez ziyada
khanjar na kisi ka hai na shamshir kisi ki
jo dil se udhar jaae nazar dil ho giraftar
mujrim ho koi aur ho taqsir kisi ki

hijr ke haath se ab khaak pade jiine men
dard ik aur utha aah naya siine men
khunedil piine se jo kuchh hai halavat ham ko
ye maza aur kisi ko nahin mai piine men
dil ko kis shakl se apne na musaffa rakkhun
jalvagar yaar ki surat hai is aine men
ashk o lakhtejigar ankhon men nahin hain mere
hain bhare laal o guhar ishq ke ganjine men
shakleaina zafar se to na rakh dil men khayal
kuchh maza bhi hai bhala jaan miri lene men

ishq to mushkil hai ai dil kaun kahta sahl hai
lek nadani se apni tu ne samjha sahl hai
gar khule dil ki girah tujh se to ham janen tujhe
ai saba ghunche ka uqda khol dena sahl hai
hamdamo dil ke lagane men kaho lagta hai kya
par chhudana is ka mushkil hai lagana sahl hai
garche mushkil hai bahut mera ilajedardedil
par jo tu chahe to ai rashkemasiha sahl hai
hai bahut dushvar marna ye suna karte the ham
par judai men tiri ham ne jo dekha sahl hai
shama ne jal kar jalaya bazm men parvane ko
bin jale apne jalana kya kisi ka sahl hai
ishq ka rasta sarasar hai dameshamshir par
bulhavas is raah men rakhna qadam kya sahl hai
ai zafar kuchh ho sake to fikr kar uqba ka tu
kar na duniya ka taraddud kareduniya sahl hai

itna na apne jaame se bahar nikal ke chal
duniya hai chalchalav ka rasta sambhal ke chal
kamzarf purghurur zara apna zarf dekh
manind joshegham na ziyada ubal ke chal
fursat hai ik sada ki yahan sozedil ke saath
us par sapandvar na itna uchhal ke chal
ye gholvash hain in ko samajh tu na rahnuma
saae se bach ke ahlefarebodaghal ke chal
auron ke bal pe bal na kar itna na chal nikal
bal hai to bal ke bal pe tu kuchh apne bal ke chal
insan ko kal ka putla banaya hai us ne aap
aur aap hi vo kahta hai putle ko kal ke chal
phir ankhen bhi to diin hain ki rakh dekh kar qadam
kahta hai kaun tujh ko na chal chal sambhal ke chal
hai turfa amngah nihankhanaeadam
ankhon ke rubaru se tu logon ke tal ke chal
kya chal sakega ham se ki pahchante hain ham
tu laakh apni chaal ko zalim badal ke chal
hai shama sar ke bal jo mohabbat men garm ho
parvana apne dil se ye kahta hai jal ke chal
bulbul ke hosh nikhategul ki tarah uda
gulshan men mere saath zara itr mal ke chal
gar qasd suedil hai tira ai nigaheyar
dochar tiir paik se aage ajal ke chal
jo imtihanetaba kare apna ai zafar
to kah do us ko taur pe tu is ghazal ke chal

hote hote chashm se aaj ashkbari rah gai
aabru baare tiri abrebahari rah gai
aate aate is taraf un ki savari rah gai
dil ki dil men arzuejannisari rah gai
ham ko khatra tha ki logon men tha charcha aur kuchh
baat khat aane se tere par hamari rah gai
tukde tukde ho ke ud jaega sab sangemazar
dil men baadazmarg kuchh gar beqarari rah gai
itna miliye khaak men jo khaak men dhunde koi
khaksari khaak ki gar khaksari rah gai
aao gar aana hai kyuun gin gin ke rakhte ho qadam
aur koi dam ki hai yaan damshumari rah gai
ho gaya jis din se apne dil par us ko ikhtiyar
ikhtiyar apna gaya beikhtiyari rah gai
jab qadam us kafirebadkesh ki janib badhe
duur pahunche sau qadam parhezgari rah gai
khinchte hi tegh ada ke dam hua apna hava
aah dil men arzuezakhmekari rah gai
aur to ghamkhvar saare kar chuke ghamkhvargi
ab faqat hai ek gham ki ghamgusari rah gai
shikva ayyari ka yaron se baja hai ai zafar
is zamane men yahi hai rasmeyari rah gai

jab kabhi dariya men hote sayaafgan aap hain
filsemahi ko batate maheraushan aap hain
siite hain sozan se chakesina kya ai charasaz
kharegham siine men apne mislesozan aap hain
pyaar se kar ke hamail ghair ki gardan men haath
marte teghesitam se mujh ko gardan aap hain
khinch kar ankhon men apni surmaedumbaladar
karte paida sehr se nargis men sosan aap hain
dekh kar sahra men mujh ko pahle ghabraya tha qais
phir jo pahchana to bola hazrateman aap hain
ji dhadakta hai kahin tareragegul chubh na jaae
sej par phulon ki karte qasdekhuftan aap hain
kya maza hai tegheqatil men ki aksar saideishq
aan kar us par ragadte apni gardan aap hain
mujh se tum kya puchhte ho kaise hain ham kya kahen
ji hi jaane hai ki jaise mushfiqeman aap hain
purghurur o purtakabbur purjafa o pursitam
purfareb o purdagha purmakr o purfan aap hain
zulmpesha zulmsheva zulmran o zulmdost
dushmanedil dushmanejan dushmanetan aap hain
yakkataz o nezabaz o arbadaju tundkhu
teghzan dashnaguzar o navakafgan aap hain
tasmakash taraz o gharatgar tarajsaz
kafir yaghmai o qazzaq rahzan aap hain
fitnaju bedadgar saffak o azlam kinavar
garmjang o garmqatl o garmkushtan aap hain
badmizaj o baddimagh va badshiar o badsuluk
badtariq o badzaban badahd o badzan aap hain
bemuravvat bevafa namehrban naashna
mere qatil mere hasid mere dushman aap hain
ai zafar kya paeqatil ke hai bose ki havas
yuun jo bismil ho ke sargarmetapidan aap hain

jab ki pahlu men hamare butekhudkam na ho
girye se shamosahar kyuun ki hamen kaam na ho
le gaya dil ka jo aram hamare ya rab
us dilaram ko mutlaq kabhi aram na ho
jis ko samjhe labepankhurda vo malidamisi
marduman dekhiyo phuli vo kahin shaam na ho
aaj tashrif gulistan men vo maikash laaya
kafenargis pe dhara kyunki bhala jaam na ho
kar mujhe qatl vahan ab ki na ho koi jahan
ta miri jaan tu kahin khalq men badnam na ho
dekh kar kholiyo tu kakulepechan ki girah
ki mira tairedil us ke tahedam na ho
bin tire ai butekhudkam ye dil ko hai khatar
tere ashiq ka tamam aah kahin kaam na ho
aaj har ek jo yaaro nazar aata hai nidhal
apni abru ki vo khinche hue samsam na ho
hai mire shokh ki balida vo kafir ankhen
jis ke ham chashm zara nargisebadam na ho
subh hoti hi nahin aur nahin katti raat
rukh pe khole vo kahin zulfesiyahfam na ho
ai zafar charkh pe khurshid jo yuun kanpe hai
jalvagar aaj kahin yaar labebam na ho

jigar ke tukde hue jal ke dil kabab hua
ye ishq jaan ko mere koi azaab hua
kiya jo qatl mujhe tum ne khuub kaam kiya
ki main azaab se chhuta tumhen savab hua
kabhi to shefta us ne kaha kabhi shaida
gharaz ki roz naya ik mujhe khitab hua
piyun na rashk se khuun kyunki dambadam apna
ki saath ghair ke vo aaj hamsharab hua
tumhare lab ke labejam ne liye bose
lab apne kaata kiya main na kamyab hua
gali gali tiri khatir phira bachashmepurab
laga ke tujh se dil apna bahut kharab hua
tiri gali men bahae phire hai sailesarishk
hamara kasaesar kya hua habab hua
javabekhat ke na likhne se ye hua malum
ki aaj se hamen ai namabar javab hua
mangai thi tiri tasvir dil ki taskin ko
mujhe to dekhte hi aur iztirab hua
sitam tumhare bahut aur din hisab ka ek
mujhe hai soch ye hi kis tarah hisab hua
zafar badal ke radif aur tu ghazal vo suna
ki jis ka tujh se har ik sher intikhab hua

kafir tujhe allah ne surat to pari di
par haif tire dil men mohabbat na zari di
di tu ne mujhe saltanatebahrobar ai ishq
honton ko jo khushki miri ankhon ko tari di
khalelabeshirin ka diya bosa kab us ne
ik chaat lagane ko mire nishkari di
kafir tire saudaesarezulf ne mujh ko
kya kya na pareshani o ashuftasari di
mehnat se hai azmat ki zamane men nagin ko
bekavishesina na kabhi namvari di
sayyad ne di rukhsateparvaz par afsos
tu ne na ijazat mujhe bebalopari di
kahta tira kuchh sokhtajan lek ajal ne
fursat na use mislecharaghesahari di
qassameazal ne na rakha ham ko bhi mahrum
garche na diya koi hunar behunari di
us chashm men hai surme ka dumbala purashob
kyuun haath men badmast ke banduq bhari di
dil de ke kiya ham ne tiri zulf ka sauda
ik aap bala apne liye mol kharidi
saaqi ne diya kya mujhe ik sagharesarshar
goya ki do aalam se zafar bekhabari di

karenge qasd ham jis dam tumhare ghar men avenge
jo hogi umr bhar ki raah to dam bhar men avenge
agar hathon se us shirinada ke zabh honge ham
to sharbat ke se ghunt abedamekhanjar men avenge
yahi gar joshegirya hai to bah kar saath ashkon ke
hazaron paraedil mere chashmetar men avenge
gar is qaidebala se ab ki chhutenge to phir hargiz
na ham damefarebeshokhegharatgar men avenge
na jaate garche mar jaate jo ham malum kar jaate
ki itna tang ja kar kuchaedilbar men avenge
garebanchak lakhon haath se us mehretalat ke
barangesubhemahshar arsaemahshar men avenge
jo sargardani apni tere divane dikhaenge
to phir kya kya bagule dasht ke chakkar men avenge
zafar apna karishma gar dikhaya chashmesaqi ne
tamashe jamejam ke sab nazar saghar men avenge

khvah kar insaf zalim khvah kar bedad tu
par jo fariyadi hain un ki sun to le fariyad tu
dambadam bharte hain ham teri havakhvahi ka dam
kar na badkhuon ke kahne se hamen barbad tu
kya gunah kya jurm kya taqsir meri kya khata
ban gaya jo is tarah haq men mire jallad tu
qaid se teri kahan jaenge ham bebalopar
kyuun qafas men tang karta hai hamen sayyad tu
dil ko dil se raah hai to jis tarah se ham tujhe
yaad karte hain kare yuun hi hamen bhi yaad tu
dil tira faulad ho to aap ho ainavar
saaf yakbari sune meri agar rudad tu
shaad o khurram ek aalam ko kiya us ne zafar
par sabab kya hai ki hai ranjida o nashad tu

kya kahun dil mailezulfedota kyunkar hua
ye bhala changa giraftarebala kyunkar hua
jin ko mehrabeibadat ho khameabrueyar
un ka kaabe men kaho sajda ada kyunkar hua
didaehairan hamara tha tumhare zerepa
ham ko hairat hai ki paida naqshepa kyunkar hua
namabar khat de ke us naukhat ko tu ne kya kaha
kya khata tujh se hui aur vo khafa kyunkar hua
khaksari kya ajab khove agar dil ka ghubar
khaak se dekho ki aina safa kyunkar hua
jin ko yaktai ka daava tha vo misleaina
un ko hairat hai ki paida dusra kyunkar hua
tere danton ke tasavvur se na tha gar abdar
jo baha aansu vo durrebebaha kyunkar hua
jo na hona tha hua ham par tumhare ishq men
tum ne itna bhi na puchha kya hua kyunkar hua
vo to hai naashna mashhur aalam men zafar
par khuda jaane vo tujh se ashna kyunkar hua

kya kuchh na kiya aur hain kya kuchh nahin karte
kuchh karte hain aisa bakhuda kuchh nahin karte
apne marazegham ka hakim aur koi hai
ham aur tabibon ki dava kuchh nahin karte
malum nahin ham se hijab un ko hai kaisa
auron se to vo sharm o haya kuchh nahin karte
go karte hain zahir ko safa ahlekudurat
par dil ko nahin karte safa kuchh nahin karte
vo dilbari ab tak miri kuchh karte hain lekin
tasir tire naale dila kuchh nahin karte
dil ham ne diya tha tujhe ummidevafa par
tum ham se nahin karte vafa kuchh nahin karte
karte hain vo is tarah zafar dil pe jafaen
zahir men ye jaano ki jafa kuchh nahin karte

kyunkar na khaksar rahen ahlekin se duur
dekho zamin falak se falak hai zamin se duur
parvana vasleshama pe deta hai apni jaan
kyunkar rahe dil us ke rukheatishin se duur
mazmunevaslohijr jo naame men hai raqam
hai harf bhi kahin se mile aur kahin se duur
go tirebeguman hai mire paas par abhi
jaae nikal ke sinaecharkhebarin se duur
vo kaun hai ki jaate nahin aap jis ke paas
lekin hamesha bhagte ho tum hamin se duur
hairan huun ki us ke muqabil ho aina
jo purghurur khinchta hai mahemubin se duur
yaan tak adu ka paas hai un ko ki bazm men
vo baithte bhi hain to mire hamnashin se duur
manzur ho jo diid tujhe dil ki aankh se
pahunche tiri nazar nigahedurbin se duur
duniyaedun ki de na mohabbat khuda zafar
insan ko phenk de hai ye iman o diin se duur

kyunki ham duniya men aae kuchh sabab khulta nahin
ik sabab kya bhed vaan ka sab ka sab khulta nahin
puchhta hai haal bhi gar vo to maare sharm ke
ghunchaetasvir ke manind lab khulta nahin
shahidemaqsud tak pahunchenge kyunkar dekhiye
band hai babetamanna hai ghazab khulta nahin
band hai jis khanaezindan men divana tera
us ka darvaza pariru roz o shab khulta nahin
dil hai ye ghuncha nahin hai is ka uqda ai saba
kholne ka jab talak aave na dhab khulta nahin
ishq ne jin ko kiya khatirgirafta un ka dil
laakh hove garche samanetarab khulta nahin
kis tarah malum hove us ke dil ka muddaa
mujh se baton men zafar vo ghunchalab khulta nahin

lagta nahin hai dil mira ujde dayar men
kis ki bani hai alamenapaedar men
in hasraton se kah do kahin aur ja basen
itni jagah kahan hai diledaghdar men
kanton ko mat nikal chaman se o baghban
ye bhi gulon ke saath pale hain bahar men
bulbul ko baghban se na sayyad se gila
qismat men qaid likkhi thi faslebahar men
kitna hai badnasib zafar dafn ke liye
do gaz zamin bhi na mili kueyar men

main huun aasi ki purkhata kuchh huun
tera banda huun ai khuda kuchh huun
juzv o kul ko nahin samajhta main
dil men thoda sa janta kuchh huun
tujh se ulfat nibahta huun main
bavafa huun ki bevafa kuchh huun
jab se naashna huun main sab se
tab kahin us se ashna kuchh huun
nashshaeishq le uda hai mujhe
ab maze men uda raha kuchh huun
khvab mera hai ain bedari
main to us men bhi dekhta kuchh huun
garche kuchh bhi nahin huun main lekin
us pe bhi kuchh na puchho kya kuchh huun
samjhe vo apna khaksar mujhe
khakerah huun ki khakepa kuchh huun
chashmealtaf fakhredin se huun
ai zafar kuchh se ho gaya kuchh huun

mar gae ai vaah un ki nazbardari men ham
dil ke hathon se pade kaisi giraftari men ham
sab pe raushan hai hamari sozishedil bazm men
shama saan jalte hain apni garmbazari men ham
yaad men hai tere dam ki amadoshud purkhayal
bekhabar sab se hain is dam ki khabardari men ham
jab hansaya gardishegardun ne ham ko shaklegul
misleshabnam hain hamesha girya o zaari men ham
chashm o dil biina hai apne roz o shab ai marduman
garche sote hain bazahir par hain bedari men ham
dosh par rakhtesafar bandhe hai kya ghuncha saba
dekhte hain sab ko yaan jaise ki tayyari men ham
kab talak bedid se ya rab rakhen chashmevafa
lag rahe hain aaj kal to dil ki ghamkhvari men ham
dekh kar aina kya kahta hai yaaro ab vo shokh
maah se sad chand behtar hain adadari men ham
ai zafar likh tu ghazal bahr o qavafi pher kar
khamaedurrez se hain ab guharbari men ham

mohabbat chahiye baham hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho
khushi ho is men ya ho gham hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho
ghanimat tum ise samjho ki is khumkhane men yaaro
nasib ikdam dilekhurram hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho
dilao hazratedil tum na yadekhatesabz us ka
kahin aisa na ho ye sam hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho
hamesha chahta hai dil ki mil kar kiije mainoshi
mayassar jamemaiejamjam hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho
ham apna ishq chamkaen tum apna husn chamkao
ki hairan dekh kar aalam hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho
rahe hirsohava daaim azizo saath jab apne
na kyunkar fikrebeshokam hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho
zafar se kahta hai majnun kahin dardedil mahzun
jo gham se fursat ab ik dam hamen bhi ho tumhen bhi ho

na daaim gham hai ne ishrat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai
tabaddul yaan hai har saaat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai
garebanchak huun gaahe udata khaak huun gaahe
liye phirti mujhe vahshat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai
abhi hain vo mire hamdam abhi ho jaenge dushman
nahin ik vaza par sohbat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai
jo shakleshisha giryan huun to mislejam khandan huun
yahi hai yaan ki kaifiyyat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai
kisi vaqt ashk hain jaari kisi vaqt aah aur zaari
gharaz haleghamefurqat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai
koi din hai baharegul phir akhir hai khizan bilkul
chaman hai manzileibrat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai
zafar ik baat par daaim vo hove kis tarah qaaim
jo apni pherta niyyat kabhi yuun hai kabhi vuun hai

na do dushnam ham ko itni badkhui se kya hasil
tumhen dena hi hoga bosa khamrui se kya hasil
dilazari ne teri kar diya bilkul mujhe bedil
na kar ab meri diljui ki diljui se kya hasil
na jab tak chaak ho dil phans kab dil ki nikalti hai
jahan ho kaam khanjar ka vahan suui se kya hasil
burai ya bhalai go hai apne vaste lekin
kisi ko kyuun kahen ham bad ki badgui se kya hasil
na kar fikrekhizab ai shaikh tu piiri men jaane de
javan hona nahin mumkin siyahrui se kya hasil
chadhae astin khanjarbakaf vo yuun jo phirta hai
use kya jaane hai us arbadajui se kya hasil
abas pamba na rakh daghedilesozan pe tu mere
ki angare pe hoga charagar ruui se kya hasil
shamimezulf ho us ki to ho farhat mire dil ko
saba hovega mushkchin ki khushbui se kya hasil
na hove jab talak insan ko dil se meleyakjanib
zafar logon ke dikhlane ko yaksui se kya hasil

na durveshon ka khirqa chahiye na tajeshahana
mujhe to hosh de itna rahun main tujh pe divana
kitabon men dhara hai kya bahut likh likh ke dho dalin
hamare dil pe naqshekalhajr hai tera farmana
ghanimat jaan jo dam guzre kaifiyat se gulshan men
diye ja saqiepaimanshikan bhar bhar ke paimana
na dekha vo kahin jalva jo dekha khanaedil men
bahut masjid men sar maara bahut sa dhunda butkhana
kuchh aisa ho ki jis se manzilemaqsud ko pahunchun
tariqeparsai hove ya ho raherindana
ye saari amadoshud hai nafas ki amadoshud par
isi tak aana jaana hai na phir jaana na phir aana
zafar vo zahidebedard ki huhaq se behtar hai
kare gar rind dardedil se havhuemastana

nahin ishq men is ka to ranj hamen ki qarar o shakeb zara na raha
ghameishq to apna rafiq raha koi aur bala se raha na raha
diya apni khudi ko jo ham ne utha vo jo parda sa biich men tha na raha
rahe parde men ab na vo pardanashin koi dusra us ke siva na raha
na thi haal ki jab hamen khabar rahe dekhte auron ke aib o hunar
padi apni buraiyon par jo nazar to nigah men koi bura na raha
tire rukh ke khayal men kaun se din uthe mujh pe na fitnaerozejaza
tiri zulf ke dhyan men kaun si shab mire sar pe hujumebala na raha
hamen sagharebada ke dene men ab kare der jo saaqi to haae ghazab
ki ye ahdenashat ye dauretarab na rahega jahan men sada na raha
kai roz men aaj vo mehrliqa hua mere jo samne jalvanuma
mujhe sabr o qarar zara na raha use pasehijabohaya na raha
tire khanjar o tegh ki aberavan hui jab ki sabilesitamzadgan
gae kitne hi qafile khushkzaban koi tishnaeabebaqa na raha
mujhe saaf batae nigar agar to ye puchhun main ro ro ke khunejigar
male paanv se kis ke hain didaetar kafepa pe jo rangehina na raha
use chaha tha main ne ki rok rakhun miri jaan bhi jaae to jaane na duun
kiye laakh fareb karod fusun na raha na raha na raha na raha
lage yuun to hazaron hi tiresitam ki tadapte rahe pade khaak pe ham
vale naaz o karishma ki teghedodam lagi aisi ki tasma laga na raha
zafar aadmi us ko na janiyega vo ho kaisa hi sahabefahmozaka
jise aish men yadekhuda na rahi jise taish men khaufekhuda na raha

na us ka bhed yaari se na ayyari se haath aaya
khuda agah hai dil ki khabardari se haath aaya
na hon jin ke thikane hosh vo manzil ko kya pahunche
ki rasta haath aaya jis ki hushyari se haath aaya
hua haq men hamare kyuun sitamgar asman itna
koi puchhe ki zalim kya sitamgari se haath aaya
agarche maleduniya haath bhi aaya harison ke
to dekha ham ne kis kis zillatokhvari se haath aaya
na kar zalim dilazari jo ye dil manzur hai lena
kisi ka dil jo haath aaya to dildari se haath aaya
agarche khaksari kimiya ka sahl nuskha hai
valekin haath aaya jis ke dushvari se haath aaya
hui hargiz na tere chashm ke bimar ko sehhat
na jab tak zahr tere khattezangari se haath aaya
koi ye vahshieramdida tere haath aaya tha
par ai sayyadvash dil ki giraftari se haath aaya
zafar jo do jahan men gauharemaqsud tha apna
janabefakhredin ki vo madadgari se haath aaya

nibah baat ka us hilagar se kuchh na hua
idhar se kya na hua par udhar se kuchh na hua
javabesaf to laata agar na laata khat
likha nasib ka jo namabar se kuchh na hua
hamesha fitne hi barpa kiye mire sar par
hua ye aur to us fitnagar se kuchh na hua
bala se giryaeshab tu hi kuchh asar karta
agarche ishq men ahesahar se kuchh na hua
jala jala ke kiya shama saan tamam mujhe
bas aur to mujhe sozejigar se kuchh na hua
rahin adu se vahi garmjoshiyan us ki
is ahesard aur is chashmetar se kuchh na hua
uthaya ishq men kya kya na dardesar main ne
husul par mujhe us dardesar se kuchh na hua
shabevisal men bhi meri jaan ko aram
azizo dardejudai ke dar se kuchh na hua
na dunga dil use main ye hamesha kahta tha
vo aaj le hi gaya aur zafar se kuchh na hua

paan kha kar surma ki tahrir phir khinchi to kya
jab mira khuun ho chuka shamshir phir khinchi to kya
ai muhavvis jab ki zar tere nasibon men nahin
tu ne mehnat bhi paieiksir phir khinchi to kya
gar khinche siine se navak ruuh tu qalib se khinch
ai ajal jab khinch gaya vo tiir phir khinchi to kya
khinchta tha paanv mera pahle hi zanjir se
ai junun tu ne miri zanjir phir khinchi to kya
daar hi par us ne khincha jab sarebazareishq
laash bhi meri paietashhir phir khinchi to kya
khinch ab naala koi aisa ki ho us ko asar
tu ne ai dil ahepurtasir phir khinchi to kya
chahiye us ka tasavvur hi se naqsha khinchna
dekh kar tasvir ko tasvir phir khinchi to kya
khinch le avval hi se dil ki inaneikhtiyar
tu ne gar ai ashiqedilgir phir khinchi to kya
kya hua aage uthae gar zafar ehsaneaql
aur agar ab minnatetadbir phir khinchi to kya

qarun utha ke sar pe suna ganj le chala
duniya se kya bakhil bajuz ranj le chala
minnat thi bosaelabeshirin ki dil mira
mujh ko suemazareshakar ganj le chala
saaqi sambhalta hai to jaldi mujhe sambhal
varna uda ke paan nashaebanj le chala
dauda ke haath chhati pe ham un ki yuun phire
jaise koi chor aa ke ho naranj le chala
chausar ka lutf ye hai ki jis vaqt po pade
ham barchahar bole to barpanj le chala
jis dam zafar ne padh ke ghazal haath se rakhi
ankhon pe rakh har ek sukhansanj le chala

rukh jo zeresumbulepurpechotab aa jaega
phir ke burjesumbule men aftab aa jaega
tera ehsan hoga qasid gar shitab aa jaega
sabr mujh ko dekh kar khat ka javab aa jaega
ho na betab itna gar us ka itaab aa jaega
tu ghazab men ai dilekhanakharab aa jaega
is qadar rona nahin behtar bas ab ashkon ko rok
varna tufan dekh ai chashmepurab aa jaega
pesh hovega agar tere gunahon ka hisab
tang zalim arsaerozehisab aa jaega
dekh kar dastesitam men teri tegheabdar
mere har zakhmejigar ke munh men aab aa jaega
apni chashmemast ki gardish na ai saaqi dikha
dekh chakkar men abhi jamesharab aa jaega
khuub hoga haan jo siine se nikal jaega tu
chain mujh ko ai dilepuriztirab aa jaega
ai zafar uth jaega jab pardaesharmohijab
samne vo yaar mere behijab aa jaega

sab rang men us gul ki mire shaan hai maujud
ghafil tu zara dekh vo har aan hai maujud
har taar ka daman ke mire kar ke tabarruk
sarbasta har ik kharebayaban hai maujud
uryanietan hai ye baazkhilateshahi
ham ko ye tire ishq men saman hai maujud
kis tarah lagave koi daman ko tire haath
hone ko tu ab dastogareban hai maujud
leta hi raha raat tire rukh ki balaen
tu puchh le ye zulfepareshan hai maujud
tum chashmehaqiqat se agar aap ko dekho
ainaehaq men dileinsan hai maujud
kahta hai zafar hain ye sukhan aage sabhon ke
jo koi yahan sahibeirfan hai maujud

shane ki har zaban se sune koi lafezulf
chire hai siina raat ko ye mushigafezulf
jis tarah se ki kaabe pe hai poshishesiyah
is tarah is sanam ke hai rukh par ghilafezulf
barham hai is qadar jo mire dil se zulfeyar
shamatzada ne kya kiya aisa khilafezulf
matlab na kufr o diin se na dair o haram se kaam
karta hai dil tavafeizar o tavafezulf
nafeghazalechin hai ki hai nafaetatar
kyunkar kahun ki hai girahezulf nafezulf
aapas men aaj dastogareban hai roz o shab
ai mehrvash zari ka nahin muebafezulf
kahta hai koi jiim koi laam zulf ko
kahta huun main zafar ki musattah hai kafezulf

shamshirebarhana maang ghazab balon ki mahak phir vaisi hi
juude ki gundhavat qahrekhuda balon ki mahak phir vaisi hi
ankhen hain katora si vo sitam gardan hai surahidar ghazab
aur usi men sharabesurkhiepan rakhti hai jhalak phir vaisi hi
har baat men us ki garmi hai har naaz men us ke shokhi hai
qamat hai qayamat chaal pari chalne men phadak phir vaisi hi
gar rang bhabuka atish hai aur biini sholaesarkash hai
to bijli si kaunde hai pari aariz ki chamak phir vaisi hi
naukhez kuchen do ghuncha hain hai narm shikam ik khirmanegul
barik kamar jo shakhegul rakhti hai lachak phir vaisi hi
hai naaf koi girdabebala aur gol surin ranen hain safa
hai saaq bilorin shameziya paanv ki kafak phir vaisi hi
mahram hai hababeaberavan suraj ki kiran hai us pe lipat
jaali ki kurti hai vo bala gote ki dhanak phir vaisi hi
vo gaae to aafat laae hai har taal men leve jaan nikal
naach us ka uthae sau fitne ghungru ki jhanak phir vaisi hi
har baat pe ham se vo jo zafar karta hai lagavat muddat se
aur us ki chahat rakhte hain ham aaj talak phir vaisi hi

tuftajanon ka ilaaj ai ahledanish aur hai
ishq ki atish bala hai us ki sozish aur hai
kyuun na vahshat men chubhe har mu bashaklenishtez
kharegham ki tere divane ki kavish aur hai
mutribo basaz aao tum hamari bazm men
sazosaman se tumhari itni sazish aur hai
thukta bhi dukhtareraz par nahin mastealast
jo ki hai us fahisha par ghash vo fahish aur hai
taab kya hamtab hove us se khurshidefalak
aftabedaghedil ki apne tabish aur hai
sab mita den dil se hain jitni ki us men khvahishen
gar hamen malum ho kuchh us ki khvahish aur hai
abr mat hamchashm hona chashmedariyabar se
teri barish aur hai aur us ki barish aur hai
hai to gardish charkh ki bhi fitnaangezi men taaq
teri chashmefitnaza ki lek gardish aur hai
butparasti jis se hove haqparasti ai zafar
kya kahun tujh se ki vo tarzeparastish aur hai

tukde nahin hain ansuon men dil ke chaar panch
surkhab baithe paani men hain mil ke chaar panch
munh khole hain ye zakhm jo bismil ke chaar panch
phir lenge bose khanjareqatil ke chaar panch
kahne hain matlab un se hamen dil ke chaar panch
kya kahiye ek munh hain vahan mil ke chaar panch
dariya men gir pada jo mira ashk ek garm
butkhane lab pe ho gae sahil ke chaar panch
dochar lashe ab bhi pade tere dar pe hain
aur aage dab chuke hain tale gil ke chaar panch
rahen hain do majaz o haqiqat hai jin ka naam
raste nahin hain ishq ki manzil ke chaar panch
ranj o taab musibat o gham yaas o dard o daagh
aah o fughan rafiq hain ye dil ke chaar panch
do tiin jhatke duun juun hi vahshat ke zor men
zindan men tukde hoven salasil ke chaar panch
farhad o qais o vamiq o azra the chaar dost
ab ham bhi aa mile to hue mil ke chaar panch
naaz o ada o ghamza nigah panjaemizha
maren hain ek dil ko ye pil pil ke chaar panch
iima hai ye ki devenge nau din ke baad dil
likh bheje khat men sher jo bedil ke chaar panch
hiire ke nauratan nahin tere hue hain jama
ye chandni ke phuul magar khil ke chaar panch
minaenuhfalak hai kahan badaenashat
shishe hain ye to zahrehalahal ke chaar panch
nakhun karen hain zakhmon ko do do mila ke ek
the aath das so ho gae ab chhil ke chaar panch
gar anjumefalak se bhi tadad kijiye
niklen ziyada daagh mire dil ke chaar panch
maren jo sar pe sil ko utha kar qalaq se ham
das panch tukde sar ke hon aur sil ke chaar panch
maan ai zafar tu panjtan o charyar ko
hain sadaredin ki yahi mahfil ke chaar panch

vaan irada aaj us qatil ke dil men aur hai
aur yahan kuchh aarzu bismil ke dil men aur hai
vasl ki thahrave zalim to kisi surat se aaj
varna thahri kuchh tire maail ke dil men aur hai
hai hilal o badr men ik nuur par jo raushni
dil men naqis ke hai vo kamil ke dil men aur hai
pahle to milta hai dildari se kya kya dilruba
bandhta mansube phir vo mil ke dil men aur hai
hai mujhe badazsavalebosa khvahish vasl ki
ye tamanna ek is saail ke dil men aur hai
go vo mahfil men na bola pa gae chitvan se ham
aaj kuchh us raunaqemahfil ke dil men aur hai
yuun to hai vo hi dilealam ke dil men ai zafar
us ka aalam mardesahab dil ke dil men aur hai

vaan rasai nahin to phir kya hai
ye judai nahin to phir kya hai
ho mulaqat to safai se
aur safai nahin to phir kya hai
dilruba ko hai dilrubai shart
dilrubai nahin to phir kya hai
gila hota hai ashnai men
ashnai nahin to phir kya hai
allah allah re un buton ka ghurur
ye khudai nahin to phir kya hai
maut aai to tal nahin sakti
aur aai nahin to phir kya hai
magaseqab aghniya hona hai
behayai nahin to phir kya hai
bosaelab dileshikasta ko
momyai nahin to phir kya hai
nahin rone men gar zafar tasir
jaghansai nahin to phir kya hai

vaqif hain ham ki hazrategham aise shakhs hain
aur phir ham un ke yaar hain ham aise shakhs hain
divane tere dasht men rakkhenge jab qadam
majnun bhi lega un ke qadam aise shakhs hain
jin pe hon aise zulm o sitam ham nahin vo log
hon roz balki lutf o karam aise shakhs hain
yuun to bahut hain aur bhi khubanedilfareb
par jaise purfan aap hain kam aise shakhs hain
kya kya jafakashon pe hain un dilbaron ke zulm
aison ke sahte aise sitam aise shakhs hain
diin kya hai balki dijiye iman bhi unhen
zahid ye but khuda ki qasam aise shakhs hain
azurda huun adu ke jo kahne pe ai zafar
ne aise shakhs vo hain na ham aise shakhs hain

vo sau sau atkhaton se ghar se bahar do qadam nikle
bala se us ki gar us men kisi muztar ka dam nikle
kahan aansu ke qatre khunedil se hain baham nikle
ye dil men jama the muddat se kuchh paikanegham nikle
mire mazmunesozedil se khat sab jal gaya mera
qalam se harf jo nikle sharar hi yakqalam nikle
nikal ai charagar tu shauq se lekin sarepaikan
udhar nikle jigar se tiir udhar qalib se dam nikle
tasavvur se labelaalin ke tere ham agar ro den
to jo lakhtejigar ankhon se nikle ik raqam nikle
nahin darte agar hon laakh zindan yaar zindan se
junun ab to misalenalaezanjir ham nikle
jigar par daagh lab par dudedil aur ashk daman men
tiri mahfil se ham manindeshama subhdam nikle
agar hota zamana gesueshabrang ka tere
miri shabdiz sauda ka ziyadatar qadam nikle
kaji jin ki tabiat men hai kab hoti vo sidhi hai
kaho shakheguletasvir se kis tarah kham nikle
shumar ik shab kiya ham ne jo apne dil ke daghon se
to anjum charkhehashtum ke bahut se un se kam nikle
khuda ke vaste zahid utha parda na kaabe ka
kahin aisa na ho yaan bhi vahi kafirsanam nikle
tamanna hai ye dil men jab talak hai dam men dam apne
zafar munh se hamare naam us ka dambadam nikle

ya mujhe afsareshahana banaya hota
ya mira taaj gadayana banaya hota
apna divana banaya mujhe hota tu ne
kyuun khiradmand banaya na banaya hota
khaksari ke liye garche banaya tha mujhe
kaash khakedarejanana banaya hota
nashshaeishq ka gar zarf diya tha mujh ko
umr ka tang na paimana banaya hota
dilesadchak banaya to bala se lekin
zulfemushkin ka tire shana banaya hota
sufiyon ke jo na tha laeqesohbat to mujhe
qabilejalsaerindana banaya hota
tha jalana hi agar duriesaqi se mujhe
to charaghedaremaikhana banaya hota
sholaehusn chaman men na dikhaya us ne
varna bulbul ko bhi parvana banaya hota
roz mamuraeduniya men kharabi hai zafar
aisi basti ko to virana banaya hota

yaan khaak ka bistar hai gale men kafni hai
vaan haath men aina hai gul pairahani hai
hathon se hamen ishq ke din raat nahin chain
fariyad o fughan din ko hai shab narazani hai
hushyar ho ghaflat se tu ghafil na ho ai dil
apni to nazar men ye jagah bevatani hai
kuchh kah nahin sakta huun zaban se ki zara dekh
kya jaae hai jis jaae na kuchh damzadani hai
mizhgan pe mire lakhtejigar hi nahin yaaro
is taar se vo rishta aqiqeyamani hai
likh aur ghazal qafiye ko pher zafar tu
ab taba ki dariya ki tiri maujzani hai

ye qissa vo nahin tum jis ko qissakhvan se suno
mire fasanaegham ko miri zaban se suno
sunao dardedil apna to dambadam fariyad
misalenai miri har ek ustukhvan se suno
karo hazar sitam le ke zikr kya yak yaar
shikayat apni tum is apne nimjan se suno
khuda ke vaste ai hamdamo na bolo tum
payam laaya hai kya namabar vahan se suno
tumhare ishq ne rusva kiya jahan men hamen
hamara zikr na tum kyunki ik jahan se suno
suno tum apni jo teghenigah ke ausaf
jo tum ko sunna ho us shokhedilsitan se suno
zafar vo bosa to kya dega par koi dushnam
jo tum ko sunna ho us shokhedilsitan se suno

zulf jo rukh par tire ai mehretalat khul gai
ham ko apni tirarozi ki haqiqat khul gai
kya tamasha hai ragelaila men duuba neshtar
fasdemajnun baisejoshemohabbat khul gai
dil ka sauda ik nigah par hai tiri thahra hua
narkh tu kya puchhta hai ab to qimat khul gai
aine ko naaz tha kya apne ruesaf par
aankh hi par dekhte hi teri surat khul gai
thi asiraneqafas ko aarzu parvaz ki
khul gai khidki qafas ki kya ki qismat khul gai
tere aariz par hua akhir ghubarekhat numud
khul gai ainaru dil ki kudurat khul gai
betakalluf aae tum khole hue bandeqaba
ab girah dil ki hamare filhaqiqat khul gai
bandhi zahid ne tavakkul par kamar sau baar chust
lekin akhir baisesusstiehimmat khul gai
khulte khulte ruk gae vo un ko tu ne ai zafar
sach kaho kis aankh se dekha ki chahat khul gai

zehalemiskin makun taghaful durae nainan banae batiyan
ki tabehijran nadaram ai jaan na lehu kaahe lagae chhatiyan
shabanehijran daraz chuun zulf o rozevaslat chuun umrekotah
sakhi piya ko jo main na dekhun to kaise katun andheri ratiyan
yakayak az dil do chashm jaadu basadfarebam baburd taskin
kise padi hai jo ja sunave piyare pi ko hamari batiyan
chuun shamesozan chuun zarra hairan z mehreanmah bagashtam akhir
na niind nainan na ang chainan na aap aave na bheje patiyan
bahaqqean mah ki rozemahshar badad maara fareb khusrav
sapit man ke durae rakhun jo jaae paun piya ki khatiyan

ghamefurqat hi men marna ho to dushvar nahin
shadievasl bhi ashiq ko sazavar nahin
khubrui ke liye zishtiekhu bhi hai zarur
sach to ye hai ki koi tujh sa tarahdar nahin
qaul dene men taammul na qasam se inkar
ham ko sachcha nazar aata koi iqrar nahin
kal kharabat men ik goshe se aati thi sada
dil men sab kuchh hai magar rukhsateguftar nahin
haq hua kis se ada us ki vafadari ka
jis ke nazdik jafa baiseazar nahin
dekhte hain ki pahunchti hai vahan kaun si raah
kaaba o dair se kuchh ham ko sarokar nahin
honge qaail vo abhi matlaesani sun kar
jo tajalli men ye kahte hain ki takrar nahin

aage badhe na qissaeishqebutan se ham
sab kuchh kaha magar na khule razdan se ham
ab bhagte hain sayaeishqebutan se ham
kuchh dil se hain dare hue kuchh asman se ham
hanste hain us ke giryaebeikhtiyar par
bhule hain baat kah ke koi razdan se ham
ab shauq se bigad ke hi baten kiya karo
kuchh pa gae hain aap ke tarzebayan se ham
jannat men to nahin agar ye zakhmetegheishq
badlenge tujh ko zindagiejavedan se ham

ab vo agla sa iltifat nahin
jis pe bhule the ham vo baat nahin
mujh ko tum se etimadevafa
tum ko mujh se par iltifat nahin
ranj kya kya hain ek jaan ke saath
zindagi maut hai hayat nahin
yunhi guzre to sahl hai lekin
fursategham ko bhi sabat nahin
koi dilsoz ho to kiije bayan
sarsari dil ki vardat nahin
zarra zarra hai mazharekhurshid
jaag ai aankh din hai raat nahin
qais ho kohkan ho ya hali
ashiqi kuchh kisi ki zaat nahin

ghar hai vahshatkhez aur basti ujaad
ho gai ek ik ghadi tujh bin pahad
aaj tak qasreamal hai natamam
bandh chuki hai barha khul khul ke paad
hai pahunchna apna choti tak muhal
ai talab nikla bahut uncha pahad
khelna aata hai ham ko bhi shikar
par nahin zahid koi tatti ki aad
dil nahin raushan to hain kis kaam ke
sau shabistan men agar raushan hain jhaad
iid aur nauroz hai sab dil ke saath
dil nahin hazir to duniya hai ujaad
khet raste par hai aur rahrau savar
kisht hai sarsabz aur nichi hai baad
baat vaaiz ki koi pakdi gai
in dinon kamtar hai kuchh ham par latad
tum ne hali khol kar nahaq zaban
kar liya saari khudai se bigad

buri aur bhali sab guzar jaegi
ye kashti yunhi paar utar jaegi
milega na gulchin ko gul ka pata
har ik pankhudi yuun bikhar jaegi
rahenge na mallah ye din sada
koi din men ganga utar jaegi
idhar ek ham aur zamana udhar
ye baazi to so bisve har jaegi
banavat ki shekhi nahin rahti shaikh
ye izzat to jaegi par jaegi
na puuri hui hain umiden na hon
yunhi umr saari guzar jaegi
sunenge na hali ki kab tak sada
yahi ek din kaam kar jaegi

baat kuchh ham se ban na aai aaj
bol kar ham ne munh ki khaai aaj
chup par apni bharam the kya kya kuchh
baat bigdi bani banai aaj
shikva karne ki khu na thi apni
par tabiat hi kuchh bhar aai aaj
bazm saaqi ne di ulat saari
khuub bhar bhar ke khum lundhai aaj
maasiyat par hai der se ya rab
nafs aur shara men ladai aaj
ghalib aata hai nafsedun ya shara
dekhni hai tiri khudai aaj
chor hai dil men kuchh na kuchh yaaro
niind phir raat bhar na aai aaj
zad se ulfat ki bach ke chalna tha
muft hali ne chot khaai aaj

dhuum thi apni parsai ki
ki bhi aur kis se ashnai ki
kyuun badhate ho ikhtilat bahut
ham ko taqat nahin judai ki
munh kahan tak chhupaoge ham se
tum ko aadat hai khudnumai ki
laag men hain lagao ki baten
sulh men chhed hai ladai ki
milte ghairon se ho milo lekin
ham se baten karo safai ki
dil raha paebandeulfatedam
thi abas aarzu rihai ki

na mila koi gharateiman

go javani men thi kajrai bahut
par javani ham ko yaad aai bahut
zereburqaa tu ne kya dikhla diya
jama hain har su tamashai bahut
hat pe is ki aur pis jaate hain dil
raas hai kuchh us ko khudrai bahut
sarv ya gul aankh men jachte nahin
dil pe hai naqsh us ki ranai bahut
chuur tha zakhmon men aur kahta tha dil
rahat is taklif men paai bahut
aa rahi hai chaheyusuf se sada
dost yaan thode hain aur bhaai bahut
vasl ke ho ho ke saman rah gae
menh na barsa aur ghata chhai bahut
jannisari par vo bol utthe miri
hain fidai kam tamashai bahut
ham ne har adna ko aala kar diya
khaksari apni kaam aai bahut
kar diya chup vaqiatedahr ne
thi kabhi ham men bhi goyai bahut
ghat gaiin khud talkhiyan ayyam ki

ham na kahte the ki hali chup raho
rastgoi men hai rusvai bahut

dil ko dardashna kiya tu ne
dardedil ko dava kiya tu ne
tabeinsan ko di sirishtevafa
khaak ko kimiya kiya tu ne
vaslejanan muhal thahraya
qatleashiq rava kiya tu ne
tha na juz gham bisateashiq men
gham ko rahatfaza kiya tu ne
jaan thi ik vabal furqat men
shauq ko janguza kiya tu ne
thi mohabbat men nang minnateghair
jazbedil ko rasa kiya tu ne
raah zahid ko jab kahin na mili
daremaikhana va kiya tu ne
qata hone hi jab laga paivand
ghair ko ashna kiya tu ne
thi jahan karvan ko deni raah
ishq ko rahnuma kiya tu ne
naav bhar kar jahan duboni thi
aql ko nakhuda kiya tu ne
badh gai jab pidar ko mehrepisar
us ko us se juda kiya tu ne
jab hua mulk o maal rahzanehosh
badshah ko gada kiya tu ne
jab mili kamejan ko lazzatedard
dard ko bedava kiya tu ne
jab diya rahrau ko zauqetalab
sai ko narasa kiya tu ne
pardaechashm the hijab bahut
husn ko khudnuma kiya tu ne
ishq ko tabeintizar na thi
ghurfa ik dil men va kiya tu ne
haram abad aur dair kharab
jo kiya sab baja kiya tu ne
sakht afsurda taba thi ahbab
ham ko jaadu nava kiya tu ne
phir jo dekha to kuchh na tha ya rab
kaun puchhe ki kya kiya tu ne
hali uttha hila ke mahfil ko
akhir apna kaha kiya tu ne

dil se khayaledost bhulaya na jaega
siine men daagh hai ki mitaya na jaega
tum ko hazar sharm sahi mujh ko laakh zabt
ulfat vo raaz hai ki chhupaya na jaega
ai dil razaeghair hai sharterazaedost
zinhar bareishq uthaya na jaega
dekhi hain aisi un ki bahut mehrbaniyan
ab ham se munh men maut ke jaaya na jaega
mai tund o zarfehauslaeahlebazm tang
saaqi se jaam bhar ke pilaya na jaega
raazi hain ham ki dost se ho dushmani magar
dushman ko ham se dost banaya na jaega
kyuun chhedte ho zikr na milne ka raat ke
puchhenge ham sabab to bataya na jaega
bigden na baat baat pe kyuun jante hain vo
ham vo nahin ki ham ko manaya na jaega
milna hai aap se to nahin hasr ghair par
kis kis se ikhtilat badhaya na jaega
maqsud apna kuchh na khula lekin is qadar
yaani vo dhundte hain jo paaya na jaega
jhagdon men ahledin ke na hali paden bas aap
qissa huzur se ye chukaya na jaega

hai justuju ki khuub se hai khubtar kahan
ab thaharti hai dekhiye ja kar nazar kahan
hain daurejameavvaleshab men khudi se duur
hoti hai aaj dekhiye ham ko sahar kahan
ya rab is ikhtilat ka anjam ho bakhair
tha us ko ham se rabt magar is qadar kahan
ik umr chahiye ki gavara ho nisheishq
rakkhi hai aaj lazzatezakhmejigar kahan
bas ho chuka bayan kasaloranjerah ka
khat ka mire javab hai ai namabar kahan
kaun o makan se hai dilevahshi kanaragir
is khanumankharab ne dhunda hai ghar kahan
ham jis pe mar rahe hain vo hai baat hi kuchh aur
aalam men tujh se laakh sahi tu magar kahan
hoti nahin qubul dua tarkeishq ki
dil chahta na ho to zaban men asar kahan
hali nashatenaghmaomai dhundhte ho ab
aae ho vaqtesubh rahe raat bhar kahan

hai ye takiya tiri ataon par
vahi israr hai khataon par
rahen naashna zamane se
haq hai tera ye ashnaon par
rahravo bakhabar raho ki guman
rahzani ka hai rahnumaon par
hai vo der ashna to aib hai kya
marte hain ham inhin adaon par
us ke kuche men hain vo bepar o baal
udte phirte hain jo havaon par
shahsavaron pe band hai jo raah
vaqf hai yaan barahna paanv par
nahin munim ko us ki buund nasib
menh barasta hai jo gadaon par
nahin mahdud bakhshishen teri
zahidon par na parsaon par
haq se darkhvast afv ki hali
kiije kis munh se in khataon par

haqiqat mahrameasrar se puchh
maza angur ka maikhvar se puchh
vafa aghyar ki aghyar se sun
miri ulfat dar o divar se puchh
hamari ahebetasir ka haal
kuchh apne dil se kuchh aghyar se puchh
dilon men dalna zauqeasiri
kamandegesuekhamdar se puchh
dilemahjur se sun lazzatevasl

nahin juz giryaegham hasileishq

nahin abebaqa juz jalvaedost

ye nukta andalibezar se puchh

mataebebaha hai sherehali
miri qimat miri guftar se puchh

haq vafa ke jo ham jatane lage
aap kuchh kah ke muskurane lage
tha yahan dil men tanevasleadu
uzr un ki zaban pe aane lage
ham ko jiina padega furqat men
vo agar himmat azmane lage
dar hai meri zaban na khul jaae
ab vo baten bahut banane lage
jaan bachti nazar nahin aati
ghair ulfat bahut jatane lage
tum ko karna padega uzrejafa
ham agar dardedil sunane lage
sakht mushkil hai shevaetaslim
ham bhi akhir ko ji churane lage
ji men hai luun razaepiremughan
qafile phir haram ko jaane lage
sirrebatin ko faash kar ya rab
ahlezahir bahut satane lage
vaqterukhsat tha sakht hali par
ham bhi baithe the jab vo jaane lage

hashr tak yaan dil shakeba chahiye
kab milen dilbar se dekha chahiye
hai tajalli bhi naqaberueyar
us ko kin ankhon se dekha chahiye
ghairmumkin hai na ho tasiregham
haledil phir us ko likkha chahiye
hai dilafgaron ki dildari zarur
gar nahin ulfat madara chahiye
hai kuchh ik baaqi khalish ummid ki
ye bhi mit jaae to phir kya chahiye
doston ki bhi na ho parva jise
beniyazi us ki dekha chahiye
bha gae hain aap ke andaz o naaz
kijiye ighmaz jitna chahiye
shaikh hai in ki nigah jaadu bhari
sohbaterindan se bachna chahiye
lag gai chup halieranjur ko
haal is ka kis se puchha chahiye

ishq ko tarkejunun se kya gharaz
charkhegardan ko sukun se kya gharaz
dil men hai ai khizr gar sidaqetalab
rahrau ko rahnumon se kya gharaz
hajiyo hai ham ko ghar vaale se kaam
ghar ke mehrab o sutun se kya gharaz
gunguna kar aap ro padte hain jo
un ko chang o arghanun se kya gharaz
nek kahna nek jis ko dekhna
ham ko taftishedarun se kya gharaz
dost hain jab zakhmedil se bekhabar
un ko apne ashkekhun se kya gharaz
ishq se hai mujtanib zahid abas
sher ko saidezabun se kya gharaz
kar chuka jab shaikh taskhirequlub
ab use duniyaedun se kya gharaz
aae ho hali paetaslim yaan
aap ko chunochagun se kya gharaz

jiite ji maut ke tum munh men na jaana hargiz
dosto dil na lagana na lagana hargiz
ishq bhi taak men baitha hai nazarbazon ki
dekhna sher se ankhen na ladana hargiz
haath malne na hon piiri men agar hasrat se
to javani men na ye rog basana hargiz
jitne raste the tire ho gae viran ai ishq
aa ke viranon men ab ghar na basana hargiz
kuuch sab kar gae dilli se tire qadrshanas
qadr yaan rah ke ab apni na ganvana hargiz
tazkira dehliemarhum ka ai dost na chhed
na suna jaega ham se ye fasana hargiz
dhundta hai dileshorida bahane mutrib
dardangez ghazal koi na gaana hargiz
sohbaten agli musavvir hamen yaad aengi
koi dilchasp muraqqa na dikhana hargiz
le ke daagh aaega siine pe bahut ai sayyah
dekh is shahr ke khandaron men na jaana hargiz
chappe chappe pe hain yaan gauhareyakta tahekhak
dafn hoga kahin itna na khazana hargiz
mit gae tere mitane ke nishan bhi ab to
ai falak is se ziyada na mitana hargiz
vo to bhule the hamen ham bhi unhen bhuul gae
aisa badla hai na badlega zamana hargiz
ham ko gar tu ne rulaya to rulaya ai charkh
ham pe ghairon ko to zalim na hansana hargiz
akhiri daur men bhi tujh ko qasam hai saaqi
bhar ke ik jaam na pyason ko pilana hargiz
bakht soe hain bahut jaag ke ai daurezaman
na abhi niind ke maton ko jagana hargiz
kabhi ai ilm o hunar ghar tha tumhara dilli
ham ko bhule ho to ghar bhuul na jaana hargiz
shairi mar chuki ab zinda na hogi yaaro
yaad kar kar ke use ji na kudhana hargiz
ghalib o shefta o nayyar o azurda o zauq
ab dikhaega ye shaklen na zamana hargiz
momin o alvi o sahbai o mamnun ke baad
sher ka naam na lega koi daana hargiz
kar diya mar ke yaganon ne yagana ham ko
varna yaan koi na tha ham men yagana hargiz
dagh o majruh ko sun lo ki phir is gulshan men
na sunega koi bulbul ka tarana hargiz
raat akhir hui aur bazm hui zerozabar
ab na dekhoge kabhi lutfeshabana hargiz
bazmematam to nahin bazmesukhan hai hali
yaan munasib nahin ro ro ke rulana hargiz

junun karfarma hua chahta hai
qadam dasht paima hua chahta hai
damegirya kis ka tasavvur hai dil men
ki ashk ashk dariya hua chahta hai
khat aane lage shikvaamez un ke
milap un se goya hua chahta hai
bahut kaam lene the jis dil se ham ko
vo sarfetamanna hua chahta hai
abhi lene paae nahin dam jahan men
ajal ka taqaza hua chahta hai
mujhe kal ke vaade pe karte hain rukhsat
koi vaada puura hua chahta hai
fuzun tar hai kuchh in dinon zauqeisyan
darerahmat ab va hua chahta hai
qalaq gar yahi hai to razenihani
koi din men rusva hua chahta hai
vafa sharteulfat hai lekin kahan tak
dil apna bhi tujh sa hua chahta hai
bahut haz uthata hai dil tujh se mil kar

ghamerashk ko talkh samjhe the hamdam
so vo bhi gavara hua chahta hai
bahut chain se din guzarte hain hali
koi fitna barpa hua chahta hai

kabk o qumri men hai jhagda ki chaman kis ka hai
kal bata degi khizan ye ki vatan kis ka hai
faisla gardishedauran ne kiya hai sau baar
marv kis ka hai badakhshan o khutan kis ka hai
dam se yusuf ke jab abad tha yaqub ka ghar
charkh kahta tha ki ye baitehuzan kis ka hai
mutmain is se musalman na masihi na yahud
dost kya janiye ye charkhekuhan kis ka hai
vaaiz ik aib se tu paak hai ya zatekhuda
varna beaib zamane men chalan kis ka hai
aaj kuchh aur dinon se hai siva istighraq
azmetaskhir phir ai shekhezaman kis ka hai
aankh padti hai har ik ahlenazar ki tum par
tum men ruup ai gul o nasrin o saman kis ka hai
ishq udhar aql idhar dhun men chale hain teri
rasta ab dekhiye donon men kathin kis ka hai
shaan dekhi nahin gar tu ne chaman men us ki
valvala tujh men ye ai murghechaman kis ka hai
hain fasahat men masal vaaiz o hali donon
dekhna ye hai ki belag sukhan kis ka hai

kah do koi saaqi se ki ham marte hain pyase
gar mai nahin de zahr hi ka jaam bala se
jo kuchh hai so hai us ke taghaful ki shikayat
qasid se hai takrar na jhagda hai saba se
dallala ne ummid dilai to hai lekin
dete nahin kuchh dil ko tasalli ye dilase
hai vasl to taqdir ke haath ai shahekhuban
yaan hain to faqat teri mohabbat ke hain pyase
pyase tire sargashta hain jo rahetalab men
honton ko vo karte nahin tar abebaqa se

dar guzren dua se bhi dua hai ye khuda se
ik dard ho bas aath pahar dil men ki jis ko

hali dileinsan men hai gum daulatekaunain
sharminda hon kyuun ghair ke ehsanoata se

kar ke bimar di dava tu ne
jaan se pahle dil liya tu ne
rahravetishnalab na ghabrana
ab liya chashmaebaqa tu ne
shaikh jab dil hi dair men na laga
aa ke masjid se kya liya tu ne
duur ho ai dilemaal andesh

kya kiya chashmeashna tu ne
dil o diin kho ke aae the suedair
yaan bhi sab kuchh diya khuda tu ne

koi puchhe ki kya kiya tu ne

khubiyan apne men go beintiha paate hain ham
par har ik khubi men daagh ik aib ka paate hain ham
khauf ka koi nishan zahir nahin afaal men
go ki dil men muttasil khaufekhuda paate hain ham
karte hain taaat to kuchh khvahan numaish ke nahin
par gunah chhup chhup ke karne men maza paate hain ham
diida o dil ko khayanat se nahin rakh sakte baaz
garche dastopa ko aksar bekhata paate hain ham
dil men dardeishq ne muddat se kar rakkha hai ghar
par use aludaehirsohava paate hain ham
ho ke nadim jurm se phir jurm karte hain vahi
jurm se go aap ko nadim sada paate hain ham
hain fida un doston par jin men ho sidq o safa
par bahut kam aap men sidq o safa paate hain ham
go kisi ko aap se hone nahin dete khafa
ik jahan se aap ko lekin khafa paate hain ham
jante apne siva sab ko hain bemehr o vafa
apne men gar shammaemehrovafa paate hain ham
bukhl se mansub karte hain zamane ko sada
gar kabhi taufiqeisar o ata paate hain ham
ho agar maqsad men nakami to kar sakte hain sabr
dardekhudkami ko lekin bedava paate hain ham
thaharte jaate hain jitne chashmealam men bhale
haal nafsedun ka utna hi bura paate hain ham
jis qadar jhuk jhuk ke milte hain buzurg o khurd se
kibr o naaz utna hi apne men siva paate hain ham
go bhalai karke hamjinson se khush hota hai ji
tahnashin us men magar durderiya paate hain ham
hai ridaeneknami dosh par apne magar
daagh rusvai ke kuchh zererida paate hain ham
raah ke talib hain par berah padte hain qadam
dekhiye kya dhundhte hain aur kya paate hain ham
nuur ke ham ne gale dekhe hain ai hali magar
rang kuchh teri alapon men naya paate hain ham

koi mahram nahin milta jahan men
mujhe kahna hai kuchh apni zaban men
qafas men ji nahin lagta kisi tarah
laga do aag koi ashiyan men
koi din bulhavas bhi shaad ho len
dhara kya hai isharatenihan men
kahin anjam aa pahuncha vafa ka
ghula jaata huun ab ke imtihan men
naya hai lijiye jab naam us ka

agar fursat mili mujh ko jahan men
bahut ji khush hua hali se mil kar
abhi kuchh log baaqi hain jahan men

main to main ghair ko marne se ab inkar nahin
ik qayamat hai tire haath men talvar nahin

ranj aur ranj bhi tanhai ka
vaqt pahuncha miri rusvai ka
umr shayad na kare aaj vafa
katna hai shabetanhai ka
tum ne kyuun vasl men pahlu badla
kis ko daava hai shakebai ka
ek din raah pe ja pahunche ham
shauq tha badiyapaimai ka
us se nadan hi ban kar miliye
kuchh ijara nahin danai ka
saat pardon men nahin thaharti aankh
hausla kya hai tamashai ka
darmiyan paenazar hai jab tak
ham ko daava nahin binai ka
kuchh to hai qadr tamashai ki
hai jo ye shauq khudarai ka
us ko chhoda to hai lekin ai dil
mujh ko dar hai tiri khudrai ka

puchhna kya tiri zebai ka

us ke jaate hi ye kya ho gai ghar ki surat
na vo divar ki surat hai na dar ki surat
kis se paimanevafa bandh rahi hai bulbul
kal na pahchan sakegi guletar ki surat
hai ghamerozejudai na nashateshabevasl
ho gai aur hi kuchh shamosahar ki surat
apni jebon se rahen saare namazi hushyar
ik buzurg aate hain masjid men khizar ki surat
dekhiye shaikh musavvir se khiche ya na khiche
surat aur aap se beaib bashar ki surat
vaizo atishedozakh se jahan ko tum ne
ye daraya hai ki khud ban gae dar ki surat
kya khabar zahideqane ko ki kya chiiz hai hirs
us ne dekhi hi nahin kisaezar ki surat
main bacha tirehavadis se nishana ban kar
aade aai miri taslimesipar ki surat
shauq men us ke maza dard men us ke lazzat
naseho us se nahin koi mafar ki surat
hamla apne pe bhi ik badehazimat hai zarur
rah gai hai yahi ik fath o zafar ki surat
rahnumaon ke hue jaate hain ausan khata
raah men kuchh nazar aati hai khatar ki surat
yuun to aaya hai tabahi men ye beda sau baar
par darati hai bahut aaj bhanvar ki surat
un ko hali bhi bulate hain ghar apne mehman
dekhna aap ki aur aap ke ghar ki surat

vaan agar jaaen to le kar jaaen kya
munh use ham ja ke ye dikhlaen kya
dil men hai baaqi vahi hirsegunah
phir kiye se apne ham pachhtaen kya
aao len us ko hamin ja kar mana
us ki beparvaiyon par jaaen kya
dil ko masjid se na mandir se hai uns
aise vahshi ko kahin bahlaen kya
janta duniya ko hai ik khel tu
khel qudrat ke tujhe dikhlaen kya
umr ki manzil to juun tuun kat gai
marhale ab dekhiye pesh aaen kya
dil ko sab baton ki hai naseh khabar
samjhe samjhae ko bas samjhaen kya
maan liije shaikh jo daava kare
ik buzurgedin ko ham jhutlaen kya
ho chuke hali ghazalkhvani ke din
ragni bevaqt ki ab gaaen kya

vasl ka us ke dilezar tamannai hai
na mulaqat hai jis se na shanasai hai
qata ummid ne dil kar diye yaksu sad shukr
shakl muddat men ye allah ne dikhlai hai
quvvatedastekhudai hai shakebai men
vaqt jab aa ke pada hai yahi kaam aai hai
dar nahin ghair ka jo kuchh hai so apna dar hai
ham ne jab khaai hai apne hi se zak khaai hai
nashe men chuur na hon jhanjh men makhmur na hon
pand ye pirekharabat ne farmai hai
nazar aati nahin ab dil men tamanna koi
baad muddat ke tamanna miri bar aai hai
baat sachchi kahi aur ungliyan utthin sab ki
sach men hali koi rusvai si rusvai hai

alameabokhakobad sirreayan hai tu ki main

shanaerozgar par baregiran hai tu ki main
tu kafekhak o bebasar main kafekhak o khudnigar
kishtevajud ke liye aberavan hai tu ki main

dhund raha hai farang aishejahan ka davam
vaetamannaekham vaetamannaekham
pireharam ne kaha sun ke meri ruedad
pukhta hai teri fughan ab na ise dil men thaam

digargun hai jahan taron ki gardish tez hai saaqi
dileharzarra men ghaughaerustakhez hai saaqi
mataedinodanish lut gai allahvalon ki
ye kis kafirada ka ghamzaekhunrez hai saaqi

ilaaj is ka vahi abenashatangez hai saaqi

ki paidai tiri ab tak hijabamez hai saaqi

nahin hai naumid iqbal apni kishteviran se
